Current Commentary

The Influence of the German Coup on the Eastern Question Is Ominous

(1) The World at the Beginning of 1933

The world economy remained in a state of panic throughout the past year. General prices and stock and securities prices were particularly low in the summer of last year. There seemed to be a turning point in July. After October, the trend shifted to a slow decline or could be said to be at a standstill. Therefore, optimists believe that the world economic panic has reached its bottom. Credit anxieties about public and private debts have gradually eased. Afterwards, they will rise again. Stockpiles are gradually decreasing. Market transactions are gradually becoming active. The market will inevitably improve day by day. At least, the direction of decline has been reversed and is a symbol of a new market.

However, for this turning point of the new market, first, investment activities must be re-expanded, and capital gains must be higher than before. Second, the market for the sale of goods must be expanded again, and its absorption capacity must be higher than today's production capacity. However, given the current situation, it is difficult to further expand the scope of investment, and there is a lack of hope for increasing capital gains. The first condition for investment activity is a mere dream. The market for the sale of goods is not a new problem that has arisen in recent years. The cause of the European War was the struggle for the market. Dividing colonies was its main factor. Today, the changes in the world can by no means satisfy even one ten-thousandth of current desires. There is absolutely no second New World to discharge surplus products. The purchasing power of cities and villages has not increased in the slightest. How can the general market be expanded? The second expansion of the sales market is also hopeless.

Therefore, the internal competitive antagonism among capitalist countries is extremely fierce. The attempt to expand territory surpasses any theoretical or ideological struggle. The Soviet Union, as a rising nation, has independently created a new system and is moving towards a socialist future, which is a spiritual hindrance to the countries of the world. The saying "Joint Offensive Against the Soviet Union" is also a superficial observation and ignores the seriousness of the conflict of interests among the countries themselves. However, all capitalist countries share the psychology of preventing "communization." Therefore, when Germany's economy was on the verge of bankruptcy and its politics were extremely volatile, Britain and France could not but find ways to reduce, and even completely stop, demanding reparations from Germany. Restrictions on armaments also had to take into consideration Germany's demands to some extent and acknowledge the principle of equality.

After Germany was extremely disillusioned, the National Socialist Party seized the middle class, held future hopes, and jumped onto the political stage to rescue Germany and create a new world order. To abolish the Treaty of Versailles and break all shackles to revive Germany is Hitler's political premise. As for the extent of its practical force today, it is feared that it will still join hands with British and French financial capitalists in secret. Politics will temporarily maintain the status quo. Suppressing communist activities is its urgent task. As for the Weimar Constitution, it still expresses its compliance. As for the change of cabinet in France, it is almost a periodic coup and is very minor in world relations.

(2) The Concept of the Powers on Japan's Invasion of China

Since the German regime has passed from the Central Party to the hands of the extreme right, logically Britain and France should express panic and take precautions. Why are they not panicked and not taking precautions? This is because Hitler's cabinet has not fundamentally denied the Treaty of Versailles and has not taken any attacking attitude towards the current system. Therefore, Britain and France can use it to resist the westward advance of the Soviet Union and seek a new balance of capitalism.

However, the credibility of the League of Nations must be strengthened to be able to subdue European countries and be jointly trusted by the world's powers. Only in this way can Germany's grievances be smoothed, the Soviet Union's agitation be prevented, and the balance of power among the great powers be maintained. Unexpectedly, Japan is forcefully advocating monopoly, regardless of everything, relying on military force, from annexing the three northeastern provinces to openly declaring military action in Jehol, directly regarding the League of Nations as nothing and our country's sovereignty as a mere formality. The reason why it is so rampant and dares to risk the disapproval of the world is that the world economic panic has not ended, and how the future will turn is still a question. The world's total production index in the past year (excluding the Soviet Union) fell by 33% compared to 1928. The major countries of Britain, the United States, France, and Germany have all fallen from 11% to 43%. This situation clearly shows that the national strength of various countries has reached its extreme exhaustion. Today's international relations are complex and intricate. International wars must be undertaken with the country's strength to cope with them. At this time, all countries are caught in extreme exhaustion. How can they recklessly start wars? And how dare they lightly start wars?

Therefore, Japan clearly knows that annexing the Northeast is the first step in breaking the international balance of power, and attacking Jehol and disturbing Peiping and Tianjin is an iron hand in destroying world peace. How can the countries tolerate this? However, they must all take into account the decline of their national economies and strive for recovery. They cannot but temporarily relax their stance on Japan's military aggression. This is why the powers have delayed and procrastinated since the Shenyang Incident one year and five months ago.

Since the German coup, the situation in Western Europe has taken a sudden turn, and the Soviet Union's momentum is growing day by day, which cannot but be worried about. If the credibility of the League of Nations is completely lost under the iron hooves of Japanese imperialism's invasion of the three northeastern provinces, not only will it be difficult for European countries to achieve a balance and any disputes will be unable to be resolved, but also the Chinese market, which bears the world's temporary hope and is the last opportunity for the capitalist market problem, if it is monopolized by Japan, the future of the world economy will be even more dangerous and the economic crisis of the countries will be even more difficult to resolve. Therefore, the League of Nations' Committee of Nineteen has a proposal to restrain Japan and advocate the denial of the puppet state. Even so, if our country cannot exert its own effective strength, even if the League of Nations Assembly resolves to abolish the puppet state, it will at most be equal to a kind of political demonstration by the major powers of the League of Nations against Japan.

Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement Approaching Expiration

Our Government Believes There Is No Need to Renew It

Beijing Chamber of Commerce Sends Telegram Requesting Announcement of Termination

(Nanjing) The Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement signed on May 6 of the 19th year of the Republic of China, with its attached table divided into two parts, Part A containing four clauses, that is, the Chinese government will maintain the tax rates to be levied on Clauses 1 to 3 of Part A within a three-year period from the date the agreement becomes effective, and maintain the tax rates to be levied on Clause 4 of Part A within a one-year period. It is now learned that the special treatment regarding Clause 4 of Part A has long expired and been cancelled, and the provisions for taxation of Clauses 1 to 3 of Part A will also expire on May 16 of this year. It is heard that the government has no intention of renewing the reciprocal provisions. (Central News Agency, 17th)

(Nanjing) The Beijing Chamber of Commerce believes that the Sino-Japanese tariff reciprocity agreement only benefits Japan, while China suffers great sacrifices. Now that the agreement is about to expire, it sent a telegram to the National Government on the 17th, requesting it to announce its termination and recover the lost rights and interests. (Central News Agency, 17th)

Legislative Yuan Passes the Examination Law and the Supervision of Examinations Law

Abolishes the Special Examination Law and the Provincial Examination Law

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 5th meeting of the 3rd session on the morning of the 17th. 71 committee members, including Zhu Hezhong, attended. The chairman was President Sun Ke, and the secretary-general was Liang Hancao. The agenda items were: (1) Report by the Legal System Committee of this Yuan on the review and amendment of the draft Examination Law; (2) Report by the Legal System Committee of this Yuan on the review and amendment of the draft Supervision of Examinations Law; (3) Report by the Legal System Committee of this Yuan on the review and amendment of the draft Organization Law of the Examination Committee. Resolutions: (A) The amendment to the Examination Law, the amendment to the Supervision of Examinations Law, and the amendment to the Organization Law of the Examination Committee were passed as amended. (B) The Special Examination Law and the Provincial Examination Law should be abolished. (4) Report by the Legal System Committee of this Yuan on the review and amendment of Articles 2, 9, and 10 of the Organization Law of the Ministry of Personnel of the Examination Yuan. Resolution: Passed as proposed. (5) Report by the Legal System Committee of this Yuan on the review and amendment of Article 4 of the Organization Law of the Examination Yuan. Resolution: Passed as reviewed and amended. (Central Dispatch, 17th)

Second Review Meeting of the Constitutional Draft Committee of the Legislative Yuan

Discussing the Constitutional Procedure

(Nanjing) The Constitutional Drafting Committee of the Legislative Yuan held its second review meeting on the 17th, with Zhang Zhiben presiding. The meeting discussed the issue of the constitutional procedure and decided to tentatively set a ten-week period, with the chairman appointing committee members to conduct research in groups. The first week will discuss issues of territory, national system, and flag color; the second week will discuss issues of people's rights; the third week will discuss issues of people's obligations; the fourth week will discuss issues of the National Assembly; the fifth week will discuss issues of balanced power between the central and local governments; the sixth and seventh weeks will discuss issues of the central government system; the eighth week will discuss issues of provincial governance; the ninth week will discuss issues of county governance; the tenth week will discuss issues of constitutional interpretation and sanctions, etc. The above resolutions will be submitted to the second Constitutional Drafting Committee meeting next week for discussion. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

(Nanjing) Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke believes that the constitution is the fundamental law of the country and is particularly cautious during the research period. In addition to appointing Dai Chuanxian, Wu Chaochu, Tan Zhen, Wang Shijie, and other consultants, he plans to hire foreign consultants from Europe and the United States to participate in the discussion, so as to draw lessons from them. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

The Sino-American Ning Case Concluded

Compensation to American Nationals Fully Paid

(Nanjing) The Sino-American Ning Case was in the 17th year of the Republic of China. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the U.S. Minister to China jointly formed the Sino-American Ning Case Investigation Committee to investigate the losses of American nationals, amounting to over 880,000 Chinese dollars and over 54,000 U.S. dollars. It was agreed that our country would repay 100,000 dollars per month starting in the 20th year. This compensation was fully repaid last October. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has reported to the National Government that the Sino-American Ning Case has been officially concluded. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

Two Iron Ore Companies in Ma'anshan Sell Iron Sand to Japan

Limin Company Punished

(Nanjing) According to reports from all sectors of the anti-Japanese association, Limin, Baoxing, and other iron ore companies in Cihu Town, Dangtu County, Anhui Province, have repeatedly collected large quantities of iron sand and supplied them to the enemy for the production of guns and cannons, which are used to kill our compatriots. According to confidential reports, enemy ships have recently gone to the area to load the iron sand. The association requests that measures be taken to stop this. The association has sent letters to the Executive Yuan and the Anhui Provincial Party Headquarters to strictly prohibit this. It has also dispatched Ni Guanghe, a member of the standing committee of the association, and Luo Tajing, Ni Huanran, and other staff members to Dangtu to discuss with the Cihu Town Anti-Japanese Association on how to stop this. After arriving at the port, they, together with Zhao Jingxuan, Chen Changming, Tang Chang, Chen Changxiang, Cha Rixian, Song Peiji, Wen Jinsheng, Li Shantong, and other representatives from the Cihu Town Anti-Japanese Association Committee, seriously negotiated with the Limin Company. Unexpectedly, the enemy ship had already left at 8 a.m. They then met with Liu Jietang, the manager of the company, and issued a warning to him, ordering him to guarantee that he would never supply iron sand to the enemy again, and fining him 20,000 ocean dollars, requiring him to remit the funds to the Nanjing Central Bank within one week for the purpose of donating to purchase patriotic aircraft. They also gave him one week to reply. It is reported that the manager of the company has submitted two guarantees on the spot, one to the Capital Anti-Japanese Salvation Association and one to the Cihu Town Anti-Japanese Salvation Association for record-keeping. He has also rushed to Shanghai to ask the board of directors of the company for instructions on how to handle this. The above is the process of negotiation with the Limin Company. As for the Baoxing Company, the representative also went to inquire, but the company has now been closed and there is no one in charge, so there was no way to negotiate. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

Rumor of Peng Dehuai's Death in Battle

Tight Security: Roosevelt Returns to New York by Special Train

Condition of Chicago Mayor and Others Unchanged

Roosevelt Talks About the Incident in the Train

National Telegram, Miami, 16th: US President-elect Roosevelt visited the injured in the hospital again today, and then returned to New York by special train. According to his remarks in the train, "When I first heard the gunshots yesterday, I was as surprised and doubtful as the public, thinking it was firecrackers. At that time, the speech had just ended, and I returned to my seat to talk with Mayor Cermak. Someone happened to bring a telegram to report its contents. I got up and leaned forward, listening to him, when the gunshots suddenly erupted, followed by a rapid succession of shots. The driver was alert and immediately started the car. I saw Mayor Cermak fall under the car, and Mrs. Gill fall a few yards away. I ordered the driver to stop the car. At that time, a detective shouted to the driver to leave the crowd quickly, and the car started again. When I ordered him to stop for the second time, someone had already carried Cermak away. I felt his wrist and realized his pulse had stopped. I was deeply afraid that he would not recover before reaching the hospital. Fortunately, he woke up after a minute. I am now especially concerned about his recovery."

Condition of the Injured is Good

Regarding Cermak's condition, he was sleeping more peacefully when Roosevelt visited this morning. The doctor said there was some hope of recovery. Although the injuries to Mrs. Gill, Sonnend, and Mrs. Cruz are severe, they are all expected to recover. The lightly injured Cadwell was mistakenly reported yesterday as a five-year-old child. Now it is known that he is a 22-year-old young man. In addition, it has been learned that there is also a detective, Clark, who was injured. This gentleman was actually the first person injured. The bullet first hit his hand and then penetrated the Chicago Mayor's chest. Seeing that Roosevelt was not injured, and fearing that the target of the assailant was the Mayor, he immediately jumped in front of Cermak, hoping to take the bullet for him. Seeing Cermak seriously injured, he temporarily stayed by his side and continued to protect Roosevelt, not mentioning his own injuries. It is said that although he was in great pain at the time, the injury was not serious. He can be described as loyal to his duty.

Sangala's Tendency to Kill is Inherent

As for the assailant Sangala, after being interrogated throughout the night, his statements remain the same. He said he was born in Calabria, Italy, is 33 years old, and apparently brought hatred with him from birth. Therefore, in school, he deeply envied classmates who were better than him. At the age of sixteen, he worked and often fought with the other boys, especially hating officials, always wanting to kill them. He was especially determined to kill all the rich and powerful people in the world, and Roosevelt was one of them. His mood was often troubled, and his desire to kill became even stronger after suffering from stomach pain. He does not belong to any party, and his actions are purely his own will. He likes to read radical literature, especially writings discussing the direct actions of anarchists. As for why he never attempted to assassinate other American officials, Sangala simply claimed that he did not have a good opportunity. Although Sangala spoke frankly and answered all questions, the police are still not satisfied with his confession and deeply suspect that such people would not seek to make acquaintances with comrades. Therefore, they are currently carefully investigating various radical organizations, anticipating that after investigation, they may find that he belongs to some dangerous group, and there are also accomplices.

Reuters, Miami, 16th: Sangala was questioned today by Professor Moray, Roosevelt's economic advisor. He said he has no interest in communism and does not understand the doctrine of anarchism.

Havas, Washington, 17th: Morgan, the captain of the American detective team, believes that Sangala, the assailant of President Roosevelt, is an anarchist, the same as Korgosweiz, the assailant of President McKinley in 1901.

The Assassination Case Court Will Open Today

National Telegrams also stated that, as for Roosevelt's attitude, it is said that he is not angry with the assailant, but is worried that there are people in the country who harbor the desire to harm officials. Roosevelt's friends want to believe that the assailant is definitely mentally ill and that his actions have nothing to do with radical movements. It is now heard that the authorities will charge him with attempted murder and, according to the US Attorney General, while there is a law against defaming the President, there is no article against assassinating the President or President-elect. Therefore, this case will be prosecuted under state law. Also, immigration officials here initially wanted to deport the assailant, but after investigating Washington, it was found that the assailant had already become a US citizen, so it is impossible to deport him. He will be questioned in court here tomorrow.

Reuters, Miami, 16th: Sangala was formally charged today in criminal court with the murder of President-elect Roosevelt and three others. The maximum penalty for each count is 20 years in prison. The defendant shouted wildly at the judge, "I don't want anyone's help. You are the judge, do what you want." After a postponement, the trial will resume tomorrow, and the best lawyer will be appointed to defend him. As for the injuries to Chicago Mayor Cermak and Mrs. Gill, the director of the Florida Electric Company, the eight lawsuits have not been added, because if one of the two, unfortunately, dies, they must be charged with first-degree murder, which could result in the death penalty.

British-Japanese Trade Competition Causes

Problems with Commercial Treaty's Existence

British Government Considers Carefully

Reuters, London, 16th: At the House of Commons meeting today, Hanmersley, the Labor Party member of parliament from Stockport, proposed that the Anglo-Japanese Commercial Treaty should be abolished due to the intense competition from Japanese foreign trade to England. Hanmersley said that unless Britain can give Japanese goods discriminatory treatment, it will be difficult to effectively curb Japanese competition. Keerwei, the representative of the Department of Commerce, replied that the British government's policy is absolutely not to abolish commercial treaties with any country. However, if the benefits of abolishing a commercial treaty are greater than the benefits of its existence, then this is not the case. All British colonies affected by Japanese commercial competition are free to unilaterally abolish the Anglo-Japanese Commercial Treaty, so there is no need to abolish it as a whole. However, the notice must be issued one year before the cancellation takes effect. Keerwei stated at the end that the matter is under careful consideration by the government.

The Situation of a Strike in France

Paris, 16th (Havas Dispatch) - The various trade associations of France had originally scheduled a strike of shops in Paris and nationwide this afternoon to protest the government's newly established tax regulations. Shops in Paris were unable to comply uniformly. The strike was fully effective in the central areas of the city, but its effect waned in the more remote areas. On the most prosperous Boulevard de l'Opéra, all luxury goods stores and barbershops were closed. All clothing stores on Rue de la Paix were also closed. The street scene was no different from a Sunday rest. On other major streets, all shops except department stores, hotels, grocery stores, and butcher shops were closed. Often, closed shops stood side-by-side with shops that remained open. As a result, those that did not strike were able to take the opportunity to profit. In the Montparnasse and Montmartre districts, where there are the most cafes and dance halls, only one-tenth of the shops closed. Generally speaking, the overall scene in the city was only slightly different from usual. The number of police officers on the streets was slightly increased to prevent unforeseen events. By evening, the majority of merchants who had not struck also closed their doors one after another, because those who supported the strike sometimes forced neighboring shops to participate, even against their will. For example, when striking merchants saw a shop open for business, they would gather a crowd of people, swarm in, and occupy the premises, preventing it from operating until the shop owner agreed to close. This was often the tactic used. However, cafes and food shops remained open until the end. In the evening, most of the lights in the bustling city shops were extinguished. Paris, which is usually a city that never sleeps, could not help but reveal a touch of desolation this time. Shops in various provinces across the country also held strikes, but daily life was not disrupted, it is said.

Another Statement by the Chinese Representative to Japan

The Spirit of the Treaty of Portsmouth

Geneva Correspondence - Mr. Gu Weijun, the Chinese representative to the Council of the League of Nations, believes that the memorandum issued by the Japanese representative on November 28, and the speeches given on December 6 and 8 at the special assembly, not only insult China but also do not conform to the facts. Fearing that the world would be misled by one-sided statements, he again described the true situation in detail, paying special attention to the secret Sino-Russian agreement, the Jinan Incident, the Communist Party, and the Manchurian issue. On December 27, he sent it to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations for reference by the member states. The original text is in English, and now the translation is as follows:

I

After the Chinese representative spoke at the Council of the League of Nations on November 21, the Japanese representative submitted a memorandum on November 28. The Chinese delegation also sent a letter to the Secretary-General of the League of Nations on December 3 to refute the points made in the Japanese delegation's memorandum. The Chinese representative also raised objections to the statements made by the Japanese representative at the two special assemblies on December 6 and 8 at the afternoon meeting on December 8. However, there are other far-fetched points in the Japanese side's memorandum and statement that China cannot remain silent about. Now, their fallacies will be pointed out one by one as follows:

On November 21, at the meeting of the Council of the League of Nations, the Chinese representative presented a book written by Mr. Goto Shimpei, "The Actions of the Japanese Army and Japanese in Manchuria and Mongolia". The book details the Japanese government's various plans to disturb the Chinese people to obstruct China's unification. In its memorandum, the Japanese representative argued that Goto was out of office when he wrote the book, and that his purpose was only domestic. However, the materials in the author's book were all collected by him during his own inspections in Manchuria or from official Japanese government documents, and the Japanese representative did not deny any of what he said. This point is extremely noteworthy. The Japanese representative also stated that at the beginning of the Republic of China, a Japanese colonel planned a restoration movement in Manchuria, and the Japanese government, after learning about it, tried to stop it. The Chinese representative did not raise this matter and expressed regret. However, the reason why the Japanese government stopped this movement is detailed in Mr. Goto's booklet. Goto said, "The royal government and Colonel Doi were not very familiar with the true situation in Manchuria, and their relationship with the Japanese rogues who specialized in disturbing China's security was not very close. Therefore, the Japanese authorities' plan to start an incident in Manchuria completely failed. However, in the spring of 1916, they were still able to gather more than 2,000 people in Dalian to form a royalist army. Unfortunately, although Japan spent a huge amount of money, these bandits and coolies could not be fully used by us." Regarding the Tanaka Memorial, the Chinese representative has spoken in detail. Now, only one point needs to be pointed out. The Japanese representative stated that former Foreign Minister of the National Government, Dr. Wang Zhengting, had allowed Japan to find a way to prevent the circulation of the document. Dr. Wang made a strong denial in a conversation with reporters from the Central News Agency on November 25. This news has been published in newspapers all over Europe. Furthermore, allowing the prevention of the circulation of this document cannot be immediately regarded as accepting Japan's denial of the document's authenticity.

In its statement, the Japanese representative stated that when the Japanese government withdrew its troops stationed in Jinan, the capital of Shandong Province, in 1927, "it received a request from General Chiang's government asking the Japanese army to continue to stay there until the government could properly ensure the safety of Shandong Province." This request is completely fictitious, and the Chinese government has never made such a request.

In addition, there is one other matter of equal importance that should be noted. The Japanese representative has admitted that in 1928, Baron Hayashi Gonsuke, Consul General Hayashi Kyujiro, and Lieutenant General Sato Yasunosuke strongly advised General Zhang Xueliang not to join forces with the Nanjing Central Government. The Japanese explanation for this attempt to obstruct China's political unification is that it was out of General Zhang Xueliang's own free will. The Chinese representative has sent a telegram to General Zhang to inquire, and has now received a reply stating, "If Japan could be so concerned about my wishes, then why would it act completely against my wishes in other matters? The fact of Japanese interference at that time is well known in Chinese and foreign official circles, and there is no need to elaborate further. If evidence is needed, there are still many written documents that can be used as proof. If I was unwilling to raise the flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun, then how could the blue and white flag be flying everywhere in the Northeast?"

In addition to falsely claiming that China has failed to fulfill its treaty obligations, the Japanese representative also stated that the National Government openly insists on adopting an anti-foreign policy. The Chinese delegation has repeatedly issued declarations and statements to explain the fallacy of the Japanese side's statement.

Now, let's present one example as proof. As of June 1, 1932, the total number of employees hired by the Chinese Customs was 8,832, of which 924 were foreign nationals, including 199 Japanese nationals. Japanese officials in Manchurian customs are also included, and almost all of them have now abandoned their allegiance to the Qing Dynasty and joined the service of "Manchukuo". However, the Chinese government has not suspended any of these Japanese officials, except for Fukuoto Juntaro, the Customs Commissioner of Dalian, who was dismissed for insubordination. The Secretary-General, whose position is currently second only to the Inspector General of Customs, is also Japanese. Is there any more obvious proof that China has absolutely no anti-foreign policy?

In its statement, the Japanese representative also stated,

"The Chinese representative pointed out the number of foreign personnel in government agencies as proof that China has no anti-foreign sentiments, which is not enough to prove anything. The Chinese government accepts these foreign personnel only because it is clearly stipulated in treaties and agreements and cannot do otherwise."

This statement by the Japanese representative not only fails to prove that the Chinese government has any so-called anti-foreign ideology, but also shows that Japan's false accusation that China cannot fulfill its treaty obligations has been refuted by its own statements. Although Japan has done its utmost to provoke trouble, even invading China's three eastern provinces, China still respects its treaty obligations. However, in terms of the friendship between China and Japan, and in terms of the disloyal fact that the majority of Japanese officials serving in the Chinese Customs have joined the service of the puppet state, China would have sufficient reason to dismiss all Japanese officials.

In its statement, the Japanese representative also stated that the majority of foreign personnel serving in the Chinese salt administration and certain railways have been expelled. This statement is also inaccurate. In order to save expenses, improve efficiency, and take into account the public interest, the Chinese government has made changes to personnel due to various reforms. However, the result of these changes is not only without any so-called "great unfortunate impact," but in fact has significant progress. Taking the Salt Revenue Audit Office as an example, on September 26, 1928, the National Government officially ordered that the office be formally placed under the Ministry of Finance. At the same time, it was stipulated that all audit offices across the country should be restored, and that if the tax revenue could not be fully allocated to the central government, at least a portion should be remitted to the national treasury for the repayment of national debt. After implementation, efficiency has been greatly improved. Finance Minister Song Ziwen issued a report on the progress of China's finances in August of this year, stating that by September 1929, the plan had achieved a great deal. The Ministry of Finance could not only pay the arrears in full each year, but also gradually repay the outstanding old debts. By the end of 1930, the accumulated interest on the British, French, and Crisp loans had been fully paid off, and the repayment of the accumulated principal had also begun. The portion of the arrears of the Hukuang loan that should be allocated from the salt tax was also fully paid off in 1931. (To be continued)

Liu Wenhui's Strategies After Returning to Chengdu

"Take Chengdu by Negotiation, Take Tong and Mian by Force"

Suppress Tian and Deng, Expand Territory

Chengdu Correspondence - After the cessation of the Sichuan War, Liu Wenhui, with no major forces pressing on the front, naturally returned to Chengdu and decided to adopt the strategy of "taking Chengdu by negotiation and taking Tong and Mian by force." Tian Songyao, who occupied Chengdu, was attacked by the Communist bandits in the rear, and Liu Xiang treated him with disdain, so he had to submit to Liu Wenhui's threat. As a result, Liu Wenhui recovered Chengdu without using a single soldier. However, Liu Wenhui's hope was not only to recover Chengdu, but also to use his entire military force to suppress Tian Songyao and Deng Xihou, forcing them to submit completely. His strategies toward Tian were: (1) to demand that Tian cede ten counties of defense area to support the 24th Army; (2) the Chengdu Arsenal should belong to the 24th Army, so as to supply machinery and ammunition to strengthen the defense of western Sichuan. His strategies toward Deng were: (1) to return the three counties of Huayang, Jianyang, and Ziyang that had been ceded previously; (2) to resolve the Huang Yin Division and the Chen Shunong Division that participated in the war; (3) the Chengdu Municipal Government under the rule of the 28th Army should belong to the 24th Army, otherwise military solutions would be pursued. Tian and Deng believed that without the support of the 24th Army, it would be difficult to resist. They could only try to make peace with Liu, but Liu Wenhui's strong attitude could not be resolved by peaceful means. As a result, Tian agreed to cede five counties to the 24th Army after the bandit suppression military operations came to an end, and requested that he not invade with heavy troops during the bandit suppression period. It is said that Liu has made considerable promises. Therefore, Tian Songyao returned to Tongchuan with a belly full of worries and anger to plan bandit suppression. As for Deng Xihou, on the one hand, he completely transferred the Chen Shunong Department stationed in Chengdu to Ziyang to avoid direct conflict with the 24th Army. On the other hand, he sent Chief of Staff Niu Fanjiu to persuade Liu Wenhui and the Baoding faction generals of the 24th Army to explain the current predicament of the 28th Army and request concessions. Deng also expressed to Liu: (1) to hand over the Chengdu Municipal Government; (2) to return the defense areas of Huayang and Jianyang counties. As for the resolution of the Huang Yin Division, it is feared that there is no way. Therefore, the Huang Division's defense areas in Pixian, Guanxian, Chongning, and other counties have begun to dig trenches to prevent the 24th Army from attacking. However, Huang Yin also went to Chengdu in person to lobby, hoping to mediate. In short, the recent situation is extremely tense. However, because of the classmates relationship among the generals of Liu Wenhui's department, most of them are unwilling to oppress the 28th Army and have also expressed understanding for Deng himself. However, Huang Yin must be given a beating. Now Deng is negotiating with Liu on the handling of the Huang Division issue. Under this pressure, Deng has not gained much benefit from befriending Liu Xiang, but has turned against Liu Wenhui. He should also deeply regret that it was not worth it. Moreover, the 24th Army has formally taken over Huayang and Jianyang counties on February 2 and 3, and will take over the Chengdu Municipal Government again in a few days. At this moment, the position of the 24th Army in Chengdu is higher than that of Deng and Tian. Especially Deng is in a more embarrassing situation. According to news from the military authorities, the issue of the Huang Yin Division has not yet been resolved satisfactorily. At present, the power of life and death of Huang Yin seems to be entirely in Liu Wenhui's grasp. Therefore, Deng Xihou's attitude is particularly passive, which is probably beyond Deng's initial expectations.

Guangxi Prepares for National Defense

The Authorities and the People are Actively Engaged

It is Expected that the Entire Province Will Be Militarized in Five Years

Nanning Correspondence - The Guangxi authorities and people from all walks of life are quite active in preparing for national defense. A brief record of recent developments is given below.

Intensify the Training of the Militia

Since the Guangxi authorities decided on the policy of "arming the people through the militia," they have been determined to run the militia and have achieved considerable results. Recently, with the urgency of national difficulties, they have intensified the training of the militia. Regarding the regular troops, in the original six militia districts, each district has twelve regular troops, and every four troops are organized into a large team, so as to be concentrated for training at any time and to be easily deployed in case of emergency. Regarding the training of the reserve troops, it has been decided to organize all three million able-bodied men in the province into reserve troops, divided into ten phases for training (each phase is half a year). Each phase will train 300,000 people. All militia budget and training rules have been compiled and are scheduled to be implemented this year. In addition, it has been decided that all soldiers in each team will be transferred from the trained militia to join the army, so that the militia and the army are integrated to realize the conscription system. It is expected that in five years, the entire province will be militarized.

Strictly Implement Military Training for Students

The Guangxi military and political conference in the 20th year resolved to implement military training in schools above the high school level to cultivate talent for officers and cultivate the people's military force. Since its implementation, the results have been good. Recently, in order to enrich the strength of national salvation, the training of the militia has been intensified. The training of the militia cadres cannot but be actively cultivated. Therefore, the government has made every effort to promote military training for students. In the high schools and above, in addition to ordering the school authorities to intensify training, it has also been found that the schools are distributed in various places, and it is difficult to supervise them thoroughly, resulting in varying degrees of progress and unremarkable results. Now, in order to rectify military training and achieve practical results, according to the location of each school, senior military or militia officers are appointed as military training supervisors. Except for the First Senior High School, which is occasionally inspected by the headquarters, Xia Wei is assigned as the military training supervisor for Guangxi University and the Fourth High School, Zhou Zuhuang is assigned as the military training supervisor for the Normal College and the Third High School, Liao Lei is assigned as the military training supervisor for the senior department of the Fourth High School, and Jiang Ruquan is assigned as the military training supervisor for the Second High School and the senior department of the Eighth High School, and they are strictly urged at any time. In the junior high schools, it has also been decided that all students over the age of sixteen will be given youth military training. The training methods have been stipulated, and the training personnel have also been assigned, and it is decided to implement it from this semester. It is found that there are more than 80 provincial and county middle schools in Guangxi Province, with about 20,000 students in total. About 15,000 or more have reached the age of military training. In the future, after the training is completed, there will be no shortage of talent for militia cadres.

Consolidate the Borderland Customs

Longzhou is an important fortress for national defense in southern China. The Fourth Group Army Headquarters and the Guangxi Provincial Government have specially appointed Li Pinxian as the Supervising Officer of Customs Affairs in Longzhou. Since the September 18th Incident, Supervising Officer Li, seeing that the three northeastern provinces were lost in no time because they were unprepared, has made every effort to manage national defense work, restoring the nine offices of the Customs Affairs Office and changing the patrol team to the Customs Affairs Police Team to maintain border security. The original fortresses, whose collapses or incomplete artillery parts have been repaired, and the organization of the fortress artillery team, and the construction of bunkers and barracks to strengthen border defense.

The People Prepare for Air Defense

For the sake of resisting aggression and defending against the enemy, the people of Guangxi urgently need to make air defense preparations to avoid being attacked by enemy aircraft. Therefore, at the January 28th Shanghai Anti-Japanese Memorial Conference, it was passed to set up the Guangxi Air Defense Committee, and the Provincial Party Headquarters, the General Headquarters, the Provincial Government, the Chamber of Commerce, the Trade Union, the Women's Association, the Student Union, the Military Academy, the Public Security Bureau, the Construction Department, the Yongning County Government, the Nanning Minguo Daily, and the Provincial Anti-Japanese Association were elected as members of the Preparatory Committee to plan all the proceedings. It is planned that each first-class county will purchase one anti-aircraft gun, two second-class counties will jointly purchase one anti-aircraft gun, and each third-class county will purchase one or two anti-aircraft machine guns. As for the detailed methods, they are still being deliberated. It is now found that the Preparatory Committee has drafted the general regulations of the Provincial Air Defense Committee, and will formally organize and establish it after it has been approved by the senior party, government, and military agencies. (9th)

Mao Weishou Goes to Northern Fujian to Suppress the Communists

Because the Jiangxi Bandits Fled to Fujian in Three Routes

Fuzhou Correspondence - The General Headquarters of the 19th Route Army held a military conference in Zhangzhou on February 7. Those who attended were Huang Renhuan, Zhang Zhen, Mao Weishou, Qu Shounian, Shen Guanghan, Zhang Yan, Tan Qixiu, Zhao Yijian, etc., chaired by Huang Qiang. The meeting opened at 10:00 a.m. and closed at 12:00 p.m. The discussions were mainly about the anti-Japanese and bandit suppression incidents. After the meeting, the division and brigade commanders returned to their original defenses. However, Huang Renhuan, Mao Weishou, and Zhang Yan took the Zhang-Quan-Fu long-distance bus to the province and arrived on the evening of the 11th and stayed at the Pacification Commissioner's Office. It is said that Huang represents Chen Jitang and is in contact with Jiang Guangnai on important matters. He will return to Shanghang to his original defense within four or five days. Mao Weishou and Zhang Yan will go to Shaowu to direct the bandit suppression, because after the Red bandits in eastern Jiangxi retreated into northern Fujian, they captured Guangze and coordinated with the Red bandits in Chong'an and Taining. Guangze is the central route, spying on Shaowu, Chong'an is the left route, spying on Jianyang, and Taining is the right route, spying on Jiangle. Fortunately, the defense line of the government army is very solid. Jianyang and Jiangle have been defeated by the 56th Division's Liu Shangzhi and Gui Zhenyuan's two brigades. On the Shaowu route, the bandits are currently engaged in fierce fighting with Ma Hongxing's regiment in Longdou, which borders Guangze. After Mao Weishou arrives in Shao, he decided to immediately command the troops of Zhang Yan, Jiang Yan, and Zhou Zhijun's three brigades to launch a second general offensive and take Guangze within a limited time to cut off the bandits' communication, and then advance into Chong'an and Taining. As for Cai Tingkai, he arrived in Xiamen from Hong Kong on the 10th and went to Zhangzhou. After dealing with the official affairs of the General Headquarters, he will come to the province. (February 13)

Large-Scale Afforestation in the Taihang Mountains

Henan Province Promotes the Afforestation Movement

The Number of Trees Planted Daily Has Reached Thousands

Kaifeng Correspondence - The Taihang Mountains are the only large mountains in North China, spreading across the provinces of Henan, Hebei, and Shanxi, with a large area. Because of the indiscriminate felling of trees over the years, the forests have been almost exhausted, resulting in mountain collapses, river breaches, and frequent floods and droughts. Those who know are worried about it. Previously, the Fifth Agricultural and Forestry Bureau of Henan Province promoted the afforestation movement by the people in the Taihang Mountains, which has been going on for two months. More than 20 enlightened rural villages near the mountains have recently gone to the bureau to receive seedlings and plant trees on their own initiative. At present, the number of people who continue to plant trees on the mountains every day often reaches about 1,000. The location is in the Jiushan area in the middle section of the Taihang Mountains, and it is said that it will be promoted from both the north and south sides. It is estimated that the Taihang Mountains are about a thousand miles within the border of Henan Province, and substantial results can be achieved in about three or four years. The general mountain people's hope of restoring the old view and increasing production is full of infinite optimism.

The Japanese Consul in Shantou Protests to the Chao'an County Government

Claiming that the Anti-Japanese Association Beat Taiwanese Merchants

Making Four Unreasonable Demands on Us

Shantou Correspondence - The Chao'an County Government suddenly received a letter from the Japanese Consul in Shantou, stating, "Xie Shidou, a Taiwanese national, aged 49, residing at No. 10 Fuxiang Lane, is a grocery merchant. At 2:00 p.m. on January 28, he was beaten and injured by members of the Chao'an County Anti-Japanese Association while selling wind ball rubber products by the side of the Xima Road in Chaozhou City," etc., and attached requests: (1) Punish the perpetrators of the Anti-Japanese Association; (2) Compensate for the loss of the damaged goods and all losses; (3) Bear the cost of reimbursing all medical expenses; (4) Guarantee that such incidents will not happen again in the future, and order the military and police to protect the Japanese people residing in Chao'an. The letter was attached with Xie's diagnosis certificate and injury bill. After receiving the letter, the Chao'an County Government immediately informed the county's Anti-Japanese Association to investigate the incident in detail. The Anti-Japanese Association immediately ordered the cadres Li Kaili and Chen Jizhi to investigate and report back. The results of the detailed investigation were submitted to the county government, and the text is as follows: "According to the investigators of the Chao'an Anti-Japanese Association, Yu Ziyi and others, the team went to Fugang on the afternoon of the 28th of last month to seize enemy goods based on reports, and did not stay in Chaozhou City. There is a warrant from the Anti-Japanese Association as proof. We went to the scene of the incident on Xima Road to investigate. According to the shop staff on both sides of the road, no one was seen fighting on the road that day. We also visited the police officer Chen Rongsheng on duty that day, and according to him, the situation was the same as before. It was also found that Xie Shidou went to the Chao'an Branch Court for injury examination on the afternoon of the 28th of last month, and claimed that he was selling children's toys on Xima Road, and that more than ten people whose names he did not know had injured the people with unknown objects. The above items are consistent with the claim in the letter that Xie Shidou was selling rubber wind balls and was severely beaten by members of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association with sticks and short sticks, and that the police at the scene stood by and did not provide protection. All the details are purely fictitious. If it was true that it happened that day, why didn't Xie Shidou, being a national of a civilized country, report to the police on duty at the scene or take advantage of the examination by the doctor in the public hospital, but instead privately went to the hospital of Zheng Yunxiang, a national of the country, to collude and create a diagnosis certificate, which is obviously a deliberate frame-up. Moreover, even if Xie Shidou was beaten, there is no accurate proof of the address of the incident, and he has not been able to provide who injured him. Since he has requested an examination from the government court, he should wait for a legal investigation and verification of what happened, where he was injured, and who injured him. Since he claimed that he did not know who injured him, he falsely claimed that he was beaten by members of the Anti-Japanese Association on Xima Road and slandered the local police. It is difficult to guarantee that he was not injured in other places due to illegal acts, or that he deliberately pretended to be injured and made false accusations to vent his personal anger. The Consulate did not investigate in detail, and only made harsh demands based on the one-sided words of the national, which is somewhat lacking in international etiquette. Before receiving the order, the reason should be to report the real situation of the investigation." The Chao'an County Magistrate Liao has replied to the Japanese Consul in Shantou based on the results of this investigation. (February 11)

Wuxi

Minutes of the Meeting of the Joint Sericulture Control Committee of Jiangsu and Zhejiang

The Joint Sericulture Control Committee of Jiangsu and Zhejiang held its first regular meeting at Xiaojishan at 3 p.m. on the 16th. The following resolutions were passed: ㈠ The draft charter of the committee was revised and passed item by item. ㈡ The plan for controlling and improving silkworm eggs was explained item by item by General Ge Jingjing, who drafted the plan. The chairman put it up for discussion. The first item, regarding administrative matters, included: (A) Investigation of problems, (B) Temporary measures for local breeds, (C) Measures for improving breeds, (D) Egg prices and grading, (E) Egg price payment. The second item, regarding technical aspects, was passed as is. ㈢ Wang Zuoquan and Shen Juru proposed a plan to promote the breeding of European-Chinese hybrid silkworms. The plan included three measures: (1) Designate sericulture agencies in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to actively engage in large-scale experimentation with European-Chinese hybrid breeds. (2) Select European-Chinese hybrid breeds with excellent results and specify appropriate quantities for breeding farms. (3) Promote the breeding of European-Chinese hybrid breeds in silkworm areas with high and dry locations. This was passed as is. The meeting adjourned immediately after the discussion. Another meeting was held yesterday. The location was changed to the Silk Factory Trade Association in Xujia Lane inside Fumen. The meeting officially began at 11 a.m. to discuss important proposals such as the Jiangsu-Zhejiang sericulture improvement implementation plan and the breeding of European-Chinese hybrid silkworms. After a lengthy discussion, all were passed as is. The meeting adjourned at 1:30 p.m.

Changshu

District Defense Training Class

Militiamen Disrupt Theater

The county government of this county previously received an order from the provincial government to organize a district militia training class in order to defend the local area. Over six hundred militiamen from all fifteen districts of the city gathered in the city on the 14th for a grand review. Commissioner Zhao Zhengping was dispatched by the province to Changshu. On that day, after the review was completed, awards were given on the 15th. The provincial commissioner left Changshu immediately. Unexpectedly, that night, over two hundred militiamen from the third, fourth, and seventh districts, all armed, went to leisurely watch a play. Upon arrival, they occupied superior seats upstairs, while the seventh district sat downstairs. The ticket collector went upstairs to sell tickets, but they ignored him. Unexpectedly, at about 10 p.m., while a double act was being performed on stage, one of the armed militiamen in the middle row upstairs, who looked like a drill instructor, first threw a teapot onto the stage and started to curse loudly. The audience was slightly disturbed, but the performers on stage remained calm. However, the armed militiamen upstairs first took away the symbols, then stood up one after another and threw teacups, teapots, and rattan chairs everywhere, causing great chaos. The audience scrambled to escape through the emergency exits, and the performance was halted. Most shockingly, some of the militiamen even threw copper kettles filled with boiling water from the tea stove downstairs, splashing the boiling water everywhere and scalding a child surnamed Mou on the mouth. At that time, due to the extreme congestion in the emergency exit, another child fell to the ground and was seriously injured by being trampled. After receiving the news, the Public Security Bureau immediately dispatched sixty armed police to suppress the situation. The drill instructor who started the trouble first escaped through the west emergency exit by climbing over the wall. The Public Security Bureau police immediately detained the militiamen from the defense training class, and County Magistrate Tan urgently ordered the district chiefs to restrain and manage them themselves. It was later discovered that the leader was Shen Ziqiao, the drill instructor of the third district. The theater then made three demands: (1) Send the leading drill instructor, Shen Ziqiao, to the judiciary for investigation. (2) The losses of the theater should be clearly defined. (3) How should the unsold tickets and audience losses be handled? Wu, the district chief, agreed to the first item. Furthermore, it was learned that on the afternoon of the 16th, Dai Liangju and others came forward to mediate and agreed to the theater's request to send Shen Ziqiao to the judiciary for investigation. However, Shen had already escaped over the wall and was waiting to be captured and sent to the county. No clear statement was made regarding the remaining conditions. The theater continued to perform on the night of the 16th.

Five Counties in Jiangbei Join Forces to Suppress Mutinous Soldiers

Over two hundred mutinous soldiers from the Jiangsu Provincial Maritime Guerrilla Unit recently roamed along the coast, wreaking havoc in the Lv, Feng, and Peng salt fields, causing great harm. Ningbo

Crowd at Competition Smashes Public Security Bureau

Residents of Zhenhai traditionally hold lantern competitions during the Lantern Festival after the lunar new year, which are very grand in scale. However, they have been repeatedly banned by the authorities in recent years, so they have not been held for seven or eight years. Unexpectedly, yesterday (the 14th), some individuals with good intentions re-initiated the event, planning to hold it for five consecutive days starting on the 14th, with all residents and businesses participating. At about 6 p.m. on the 14th, everyone gathered at the parade ground, preparing to set off on a parade. For a time, viewers gathered, and the road became blocked. The County Public Security Bureau learned of the matter and immediately sent a team to stop it. At this time, it could have been resolved peacefully. Unexpectedly, a group of vagrants incited the crowd, who swarmed to the front of the Public Security Bureau and made a great disturbance. They then carried out a riot, destroying eleven rooms in the bureau chief's office, police dormitory, kitchen, and detention center. Two offenders in the detention center took the opportunity to escape. The bedding, clothes, boxes, and baskets in the chief's office and police dormitory were all destroyed or stolen by hooligans, and nothing remained. Subsequently, the First Garrison Battalion arrived, and the rioters, seeing the unfavorable situation, began to disperse.

Rioters Rampage on Daishan Island

The Donghai轮 (Donghai Ship) of the Ningbo Shipping Bureau in Yongbu (Ningbo) departed from Daishan on the morning of the 14th at 8 am, carrying cargo and passengers. At 5 pm in the evening, it arrived at the Gaoting waters more than ten li from Daishan. Suddenly, a small boatman reported that there were seventy to eighty rioters rampaging on Daishan, and the local people were deeply worried. After receiving the news, the ship dared not move forward and immediately returned to Yongbu. In addition, the Xin Sanbei 轮 (New Sanbei Ship) of the Sanbei Company departed from Shenjiamen for Yongbu at 5 am on the 15th. When it passed the Qingyantou port surface, more than eight li away from Zhoushan, seven or eight rioters suddenly came from the left bank, first fired shots to demonstrate, and then ordered the ship to stop. Seeing the bad situation, the shipowner immediately opened the accelerator and fled. The rioters fired shots, and one bullet hit the third-class cabin of the ship at the time, piercing six deck planks and falling into the dining room. Fortunately, no one was injured. In addition, the Dazing small ship, which was sailing between Daishan and Shenjiamen, had been robbed and used by the rioters. On the afternoon of the 14th, after the merchants in Shenjiamen learned of the alarming news from Daishan, people were panicked, and the market closed early. However, it is still impossible to find out where the rioters came from and the extent to which Daishan was ravaged by bandits. However, according to general speculation, the rioters should be part of the mutinous soldiers of Liu Zhennian's division in Taigu County, Wenzhou.
