Local News

George Bernard Shaw Passed Through Shanghai Yesterday Heading North

Soong Ching-ling Welcomed Him, Sun Yat-sen's Residence Hosted a European-Style Banquet Yesterday Afternoon

Afternoon Literary Gathering Held at the World Academic Society

Shaw Met with Reporters and Gave Insightful and Witty Remarks

Stating that Britain Basically Has No Policy Towards China

The British literary giant George Bernard Shaw and his wife, traveling the world on the Changxing Company's British Queen Ship, arrived at Wusongkou from Hong Kong at six o'clock yesterday morning. Mr. Shaw transferred to a customs small ship, which was chartered by Madame Soong Ching-ling and others, to welcome him. He landed at the Yangshupu Lan Road pier at 10:30 a.m.

Immediately at noon, he went to Madame Sun's residence for a banquet. At 2:30 p.m., he went to the World Academic Society to attend a gathering hosted by the literary association. At 3 p.m., he returned to Sun's residence to meet with Chinese and foreign reporters. At 6 p.m., he returned to the original ship and left Shanghai at 11 p.m. heading north directly to Qinhuangdao. He is the honorary chairman of the World Anti-Imperialist League and a socialist believer. When talking with reporters, he showed off his eloquence, speaking fluently and incessantly, interspersed with humorous satire and insightful remarks. He spoke highly of Soviet Russia and said that the whole world would eventually converge on the same path and realize socialism sooner or later. The following is a detailed account of his arrival in Shanghai and his remarks.

Welcome and Slogans

Yesterday morning, those who went to the pier to welcome him in succession included representatives from the China Film Culture Association, the Shanghai Theater Troupe Federation, Hong Shen, Ying Yunwei, the Shanghai Student Theater Society Aid Righteous Army Entertainment Conference Delegation, and four hundred young men and women who admired Shaw, each holding welcome flags and raising welcome slogans for Shaw, eagerly hoping to catch a glimpse of Shaw's demeanor and express their sincere intentions. Lin Yutang, Shao Xunmei, and more than twenty Chinese and foreign journalists from the People's Rights Protection League also waited for Shaw to arrive for an interview. From 6 a.m. to over 12 noon, their enthusiasm did not diminish, and the enthusiastic scene was rarely seen in the past. The Shanghai Student Theater Society Aid Righteous Army Entertainment Conference also issued a declaration to welcome Shaw to Shanghai. The final slogans were as follows: Welcome Revolutionary Artist George Bernard Shaw, Welcome Playwright George Bernard Shaw, Welcome God of Peace George Bernard Shaw, Welcome Shaw Who Sympathizes with China's Territorial Integrity, Welcome Shaw Who Sympathizes with China's Independence and Liberation, Welcome Shaw, Vanguard of Anti-Imperialism, Welcome Shaw to Overthrow Imperialism, Welcome Shaw to Oppose Japanese Aggression in North China, Welcome Shaw to Oppose the Second World War, Welcome Shaw Not to Be a Laggard of the Times.

Soong Ching-ling Welcomed Him

Madame Soong Ching-ling and Shaw are both honorary chairmen of the World Anti-Imperialist League. Therefore, Madame Sun, accompanied by Yang Xingfo and others, took the Jinghan small ship from Xinkai Pier at 5 o'clock yesterday morning and sailed to Wusongkou to welcome him. The water patrol team dispatched many water police officers to escort the ship. At that time, many news reporters and Hong Shen and others, representatives of the Theater Association, also planned to attach themselves to the ship, but they were all refused, saying that this was a special ship and did not carry other passengers.

Quietly Landed Together

Madame Sun arrived at Songkou at 6:45 a.m., boarded the British Queen Ship, visited Mr. Shaw, and was very happy to see him. Mr. Shaw immediately invited Madame Sun to sit opposite him in the dining room and have breakfast together. Mr. Shaw was already seventy-seven years old, but he had a youthful face and white hair, and he was full of energy. Mr. Shaw originally intended not to land due to Madame Sun's illness, but at Madame Sun's strong request, his interest in traveling was renewed. At the time, all parties were waiting to welcome him at the Xinguang Wharf, but Mr. Shaw quietly landed with Madame Soong Ching-ling at the Yangshupu Wharf at 10:30 a.m., hired a streetcar, and went to Sun's residence at 29 Moliere Road to rest. The welcoming staff did not return sadly until they received a telephone report from the water police.

Mr. Shaw photographed at Sun's residence (photographed by Li Zunyong)

Visited Cai Yuanpei

After Mr. Shaw and Madame Sun landed, they first went to the Richard Hotel on the Bund to meet with members of various tourist groups who had also come to Shanghai. After a brief greeting, they went to Albert Road to visit Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica. At twelve o'clock, they went to Sun's residence to attend Madame Sun's lunch, which was Chinese cuisine. Those who accompanied him were Cai Yuanpei, Yang Xingfo, Lin Yutang, and Yi Luosheng, etc. At about 2 p.m., this white-haired and silver-bearded literary giant, full of energy, accompanied by Lin Yutang, Cai Yuanpei, and Yang Xingfo, etc., suddenly came out of Sun's residence with smiles on their faces, got into a car, and went to the World Academy to attend a gathering hosted by the literary association.

Mei Lanfang Attended

When Mr. Shaw and others arrived at the World Academic Society, Mei Lanfang, Ye Gongchuo, Zhang Xinhai and his wife, Shao Xunmei, and Miss Tang Ying, etc., had already arrived. Zhang Xinhai introduced them one by one and shook hands with Shaw as a courtesy. When introducing Mei Lanfang, Mr. Shaw talked with him for a long time, with Zhang Xinhai translating. Mr. Shaw said that British dramas do not have the sound of iron drums, etc. As soon as there is noise during the performance, it will damage the audience's attention. However, Chinese dramas are quite accustomed to noise. Mei replied that there are two types of Chinese dramas, such as Kunqu, which is not noisy. Mr. Ye Gongchuo immediately said that Mr. Mei's performances do not have noise, and if there is, it is only the assistance of music. Mr. Mei then expressed his admiration and said that he has been living on stage for thirty years and has always known that Irish people are full of loyalty and friendship. In the future, he would like to get to know Mr. Shaw and become a friend. When Shaw heard that Mr. Mei had been living on stage for thirty years, he stared at his face and said, "You truly have the art of staying young." After talking with Mr. Mei, Shaw stood up and made a humorous speech, the main points of which are as follows: "A speech is not necessary at this moment, because everyone here is a writer. I am truly showing off my axe in front of the door. Ordinary people regard writers as mysterious and great figures. Now that you all know the content, what is the point of saying more? Moreover, writers are actually laborers, but their wages are less than those of laborers." At this time, Lin Yutang said to Shaw, "Sir, you may not be entirely right." (Because the royalties drawn from Mr. Shaw's books in the UK are particularly heavy.) Shaw replied that not all of my works have income. (According to Shaw's practice, small books or speeches on social issues are not charged.) Moreover, my plays earn money and are all given to me by the actors. Mr. Mei, who is present, can prove that this statement is true. Shaw then said, "I am here like an exhibit in a zoo. Everyone has seen it, and I don't need to say more." After the speech, Ye Gongchuo asked Shaw why he didn't eat meat. Shaw said, "I don't need a reason. I don't like to eat meat, so I don't eat meat." Later, the literary association gave Shaw a set of theatrical ghost masks made of mud from the Dong'an Market in Beijing, in a brocade box, along with an ancient embroidered robe. After appreciating them, he sighed and said, "There are different roles in the play, such as warriors, old men, young men, actresses, and demons, which can all be distinguished from their faces. However, our faces are mostly the same, but our inner nature may not be similar." His words were very humorous and thought-provoking.

Mr. Shaw photographed when he left the World Society (photographed by Li Zunyong)

Impressions of China

Mr. Shaw left the World Society at about 3 p.m. and returned to Sun's residence on Moliere Road. He then met with reporters from various Chinese and foreign newspapers in the garden of Sun's residence. The reporters first asked Mr. Shaw about his impressions of China on this trip. Shaw shrugged his shoulders, smiled, and said that the answer to this question cannot be fully described in one or two short phrases, just like an author writing a huge work of more than twenty volumes, which cannot be completed in a short time. Shaw said that he is seventy-seven years old this year. Whenever he arrives in various parts of the world and encounters news reporters, he must be asked this question, whether in cold or tropical regions. In fact, the phenomenon of the world is always like this. Moreover, he has only arrived in China for a short time, so he does not have a complete impression to describe.

No Culture to Speak Of

Secondly, Shaw also criticized the shortcomings of Chinese culture. He said that China and the East have no culture to speak of. The meaning of culture, as explained by science, is everything human behavior that can increase human happiness, especially the control of nature. In China, apart from the fields and villages, a little culture can be found, but otherwise there is no culture to speak of. Today, China is moving many so-called "cultures" from Western Europe that have lost their effectiveness and harm the public. For example, the rise of parliament is because people do not want a government. The British people used parliament, first to overthrow the rule of the emperor, and then to overthrow the authority of the church, but in the end, they never overthrew the power of capital, because it was controlled by capital. In addition, British universities almost completely destroy the individual's free will and instill outdated and useless antiques into the minds of students, making them into figures with a certain format. What will happen at a certain time, what reaction will there be in a certain situation, can be predicted and determined. What is the benefit of China moving such so-called Western culture?

Oppressed Nations

The reporter then asked how the oppressed nations of the East can find a way out. Shaw thought for a while and replied that it is difficult to answer the above question. It is better to wait until he leaves Shanghai before answering, because it does not seem very safe to speak here. At that time, another reporter questioned Shaw, saying that this kind of answer is of little help to China. Shaw then explained in detail, and also mentioned the collapse of capitalism, the spirit of Marxism, and the methods of the Soviet Russian revolution, talking endlessly.

Describe Revolutionary Methods

Once Shaw started on a question, he would talk endlessly. Therefore, from the above question of the way out for small and weak nations, he unconsciously talked about the question of revolutionary methods. Shaw said that when he passed through Hong Kong, he had instructed students to revolt, but please do not misunderstand, he did not advise students to beat the police on the street. When the police hold their guns to suppress them, the most appropriate method is to run away, and run away as soon as possible, so as not to have their heads broken and bleed. There is no need to confront the police, because the police are like a pistol in the hands of a robber. We never want to confront the pistol when we encounter a robber, but we want to defeat the person holding the gun. This requires organization and planning, and cannot be done by brute force. That is, if the workers strike to demand treatment, the result will inevitably be freezing and starvation. From the standpoint of socialism, I oppose strikes, but in today's environment, this method sometimes has to be adopted.

Praised Soviet Russia

He then said that in recent years, the internal phenomena of Soviet Russia, both spiritually and materially, have shown good and sufficient performance. This kind of large-scale progress not only benefits Soviet Russia itself and achieves complete success, but also serves as a good example for other countries to learn from, imitate, and implement. Shaw also firmly expressed his observation that he believes that socialism will eventually be universally implemented in all countries in the world. Although the means and steps of the revolution may be different in each country, they will eventually converge on the same path and become a horizontal line. As for the success of the Soviet Russian revolution, it can also be said to be due to the fact that the treatment of political prisoners in the era of the Russian imperial system was too harsh, driving those with different political ideas to Siberia, which happened to unite a group of resolute people with revolutionary sentiments and gave them the opportunity to read, think deeply, research, and organize. At that time, a Russian newspaper reporter who was present suddenly said to Shaw that what he saw in Russia when he left the country was nothing but chaos, and it was not as praised as he said. Then Shaw resolutely told him that what you said was what you saw when you left Russia in 1922, not the recent situation in Soviet Russia. If you return to the country to observe at this time (if you can still escape after returning to the country today), you will know that the current situation is very good. Judging the current Soviet Russia based on past observations, of course, you cannot know the speed of recent progress in Soviet Russia.

British Policy Towards China

The reporter then asked what Britain's policy towards China was. Shaw smiled and replied that it can be said that no one in Britain knows China, so there is no policy to talk about. He also said that the Lytton Report can be said to be fair, but it is too long and I am afraid that no one can read it all thoroughly. Shaw paused at this point and then said that today Britain itself has so many problems that need to be resolved urgently that it has no time to ask about China again.

Need is Practical

He also said that what China needs today is a good government. We must know that good governments and good officials are never welcome by the general public. Chinese politics often suffer from too much talk and no real effect. Therefore, the most needed thing is practical work.

Shanghai is Very Bad

Finally, the reporter asked what he thought of Shanghai. Shaw said that Shanghai is very bad. He also asked what he thought of the Second World War. According to the answer, we can wait for the Second World War to come. There is no need to worry about it today. They talked for about forty-five minutes. The reporter saw that Shaw was showing signs of fatigue, so they said goodbye to each other. Shaw then talked briefly with Song and others, and at 4:30, he was accompanied by Madame Sun and Yang Xingfo to the pier and took a ferry to Wusong to board the British Queen Ship. Madame Sun and others did not return home until about 8 o'clock. Mr. Shaw and his wife also set sail at 11 o'clock that night and sailed to Qinhuangdao.

Weng Zhao-yuan's Letter to Shaw

The British contemporary literary giant George Bernard Shaw came to Shanghai and visited the Shanghai battlefield. Weng Zhao-yuan, a famous anti-Japanese general, specially asked Yin Zhiling to represent him in welcoming him and presented him with a copy of the English-language "Memoirs of the Bloody Battle of Shanghai" and sent a letter to Shaw saying, "Dear Mr. Shaw, I am pleased to hear that you have come to China and visited the site of the January 28th Shanghai War. I am sorry that I cannot accompany you because I am away from Shanghai. I would like to present you with a copy of my English-language "Memoirs of the Bloody Battle of Shanghai" as a souvenir of your visit to China. I would also like you to see the remnants of the artillery fire of the strong after seeing them in person, and then read this book, so that you can know the touching and admirable situation of the oppressed people fighting bloody battles at that time. I would also like to ask you to be a contemporary literary giant, who usually vomits his blood and writes out the philosophy of mankind's love of life and hatred of death, and leads the people to embark on the road of peace. How can you know that in this world where the East and the West are competing for civilization, there are still such fierce people in the Far East who show their ferocious faces and cruel methods and regard human peace as worthless? In that case, since you have come to this place and know this situation, how much more compassionate tears will you shed for these human beings? I hope you will take care of yourself. Respectfully, Weng Zhao-yuan."

The Water Cut-Off Problem is Serious

The Real Estate Association Decided to Refuse to Pay Water Bills

Tragic Accidents Occurred in Both Pudong and Puxi Due to Water Cut-Offs Yesterday

Representatives of the Real Estate Association Will Petition the Municipal Government Today

The Guowen News Agency reported that within the Public Concession, the water company, disregarding everything, has implemented a water cut-off, which has already caused a city-wide storm. Yesterday morning, in Sanxingfang, Tangshan Road, Pudong, a death occurred due to a dispute over water after the water was cut off. In Yidingpan Road, Puxi, tragic incidents such as the explosion of steam boiler water tanks also occurred due to the water cut-off. The Real Estate Association, after a general meeting yesterday, decided to notify its members to refuse to pay water bills from now on in order to deal with the situation. The following is a record of the various situations:

Representatives Attending

Those who attended the meeting yesterday included companies such as Yizhongyin Company, Deli, Jingji, Jiuxing, Chengyu, Longzhang, Xingji, Central Trust, Changtai, Taili, Xinghe Business, Fenxing, Hexing, Yuji, Yude, Qinyu, Tongde, Huada, Changfeng, Renxin, Jingji, Haufeng Real Estate, Hekun Trust, Xielong Real Estate, Sanxin, Yongqing, etc., and Shenyutang, Gu Lanji, World Book Company, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Xu Xiangji, Dali Accounting Firm Real Estate Department, Zhou Gengji, Yunji, Shanghai Bank, Continental Bank, and other leasing accounting firms and real estate department representatives, totaling more than two hundred people.

Important Matters Resolved by the General Meeting

After the representatives arrived one after another, the meeting was announced to begin promptly at four o'clock. Chairman Kui Yanfang first gave a report, stating roughly: For forty-five years, the water company has been charging at a rate of five percent. In the past two years, they have increased water rates twice, using the high value of gold and low value of silver as a justification for the price increase. We have questioned them as to why they did not reduce water rates when silver was expensive and gold was cheap. The report by the American, Hill, who came to Shanghai to investigate, did not clearly understand the facts, so the results still lacked effective solutions. Now, the water company is using the appalling means of cutting off water, which is truly an act of murder. The mask of their being a civilized nation has been completely torn off. The partiality of the Public Works Department towards the water company is evident, as they have even sent police to protect the water shut-offs. In short, regardless of what happens, if water rates are increased again, landlords and tenants will have no way to survive. We can only strive hard to achieve the goal of abolishing meter installations, and more. Next, he reported on the progress of negotiations with various parties (details omitted). Attendees, including Shen Jixuan, Wu Wenyuan, Ye Shantao, Xiao Zonghan, Chen Chenggang, and others, successively stood up, expressed their opinions, and discussed for over two hours. The chairman summarized the opinions and resolved the following important matters: ㈠ It was decided to appoint Kui Yanfang, Shen Jixuan, Li Bohan, Guo Zusheng, Xiao Zonghan, Wu Wenyuan, Zhao Ziyu, Lu Hanting, and others to go to the municipal government together this afternoon at two o'clock to petition, requesting the Public Concession authorities to stop the Shanghai Water Company's murderous act of cutting off water supply. ㈡ Before the water company resumes supplying the water that has been cut off and sincerely seeks a reasonable and legal solution, all water fees will be withheld and not paid. A notice will be published in the newspaper to inform the real estate industry throughout the city to implement this. Finally, other matters were discussed, and the meeting adjourned.

Notice to Suspend Water Fee Payments

The Shanghai Real Estate Association, after a meeting resolution, published the following notice: Urgent Announcement: The Shanghai Water Company in the Public Concession, seeking unilateral benefits, disregards the affordability of the citizens and uses the means of cutting off water to coerce and collect huge and escalating water fees calculated by meter, causing citizens to face the danger of being unable to cook or drink, endangering their lives. The water company has placed the lives of the citizens outside of consideration. To alleviate the danger to the livelihoods of the citizens, this association unanimously resolved at the meeting on the seventeenth of this month that before the Shanghai Water Company resumes supplying the water that has been cut off and sincerely seeks a reasonable and legal solution, all water fees will be withheld and not paid. Because the matter concerns the lives and safety of the citizens, this urgent announcement is hereby issued. We respectfully request everyone's united assistance in implementing this. Your kind attention is appreciated.

Questioning Armed Water Shutoffs

The Shanghai Real Estate Association sent a letter yesterday to Zhong Siyun, the Director-General of the Shanghai Public Works Department in the Public Concession. It reads: Dear Sir, According to a letter from our member, Xie Xing Company, the main water pipe in Weishui Fang on Zhejiang Road was cut off by the British-owned Shanghai Water Company at 4:15 PM on February 13th. Four workers, two foreign staff members, and one Chinese and one Western patrolman from the police, (all wearing coats that covered the numbers on their uniforms), provided protection during the operation. Furthermore, a letter from Qin Yu Company states that at 10:00 AM on February 15th, the British-owned Shanghai Water Company dispatched several workers, foreign staff, and numerous Chinese and Western patrolmen to Qin Yu Li on Linqing Road, Yangshupu, where they cut off the water pipe in the neighborhood. Additionally, a letter from Huada Real Estate Company claims that at 12:00 PM on February 14th, the British-owned Shanghai Water Company, along with several foreign staff members and Chinese and Western detectives, cut off the main water pipe at the entrance of Shunzhi Li on Kunming Road. Furthermore, a report from Jing Ji Company states that at 10:00 AM on February 15th, the water company cut off the main water pipe in Sanxing Fang on Tangshan Road. These reports have reached our association. Given that the water issue is currently under discussion by the Public Utilities Committee and the Board of Directors for a reasonable solution, the water company's continued water shutoffs and refusal to reconnect the water demonstrate a lack of concern for public safety and disregard for your department, which is abundantly clear. Public opinion widely believes that your department is an agency authorized by taxpayers to protect the safety of their lives and property and must step forward to correct the water company's arbitrary behavior to fulfill its due responsibility. In the past, the water company often claimed that the water shutoffs were approved by your department. The public generally regarded this as a pretext for the water company to shirk responsibility. In light of the aforementioned three water shutoffs, where Chinese and Western detectives were present on site, it is clear that the water shutoffs are being implemented jointly by the police, or at least those with the authority to command the patrolmen, and the water company. This situation is causing the public to mistakenly believe that the patrolmen are acting as the water company's police, rather than protecting the safety of taxpayers' lives and property. If this is a misunderstanding of the latter kind, the harm is relatively small, and it would be sufficient for your department to issue a formal statement and investigate the patrolmen involved. However, if it is a misunderstanding of the former kind, it will lead people to suspect that the patrolmen are the water company's police, not those who protect, but rather those who destroy the safety of taxpayers' lives and property. In that case, those responsible for the harm caused by the water shutoffs will include not only the water company but also others. Regarding the information provided in this letter, we hereby request that you, Director-General, provide a clear response to avoid public misunderstanding and prevent the water issue from becoming even more complicated. This is our sincere hope.

Urging the Director-General to Reflect

Hou Xing Real Estate Company sent a letter yesterday to the Real Estate Association, stating: Yesterday, we received your instructions and learned that our company's houses in Weishui Fang on Zhejiang Road are paying water fees according to a water-inclusive contract. We have repeatedly requested your association to urge the water company to collect the fees on a monthly basis and stated that the company should be responsible for any delays. Later, we sent the water fees for June to November, calculated according to the signed water-inclusive contract, totaling 1,336.5 taels of silver, to the company, which accepted it and issued a receipt as proof of the contractual arrangement. This is a common practice for both Chinese and foreign parties. However, on the afternoon of the 13th of this month, the Public Works Department sent police to forcibly cut off the main water pipe together with the water company, disregarding the lives of the citizens. Was the Public Works Department established to maintain local security, or is it a profit-making agency for the water company? Director-General Jones's one-sided hearing and defense are baffling. May we ask, who is the Director-General being paid by? Please forward all past correspondence regarding the negotiations, as well as the payment of water fees and the reminders we sent, to the Director-General for his review, so that he can immediately reflect and start thinking about the citizens' welfare.

Two Cases of Fatal Injuries

Following the water shutoffs by the water company, two cases of fatal injuries occurred yesterday morning in Pudong and Puxi, respectively. The circumstances are as follows: ㈠ In Sanxing Fang on Tangshan Road, Pudong, the entire neighborhood consists of 107 buildings, with a population of over 2,000, mostly working-class residents. Recently, the neighborhood's water supply has been cut off. Residents have been taking water from the public tap to sustain their lives. However, yesterday morning around 11:00 AM, a resident of the neighborhood, Jiao Liang, a woman from Tianjin, suddenly got into an argument with a woman from Shandong over water. The argument escalated into a physical fight, and the woman from Tianjin severely injured the Shandong woman in the head and waist. Onlookers apprehended the attacker and handed her over to the police. The injured woman was taken to the hospital for treatment. Her injuries are said to be severe, and her life is in danger. ㈡ At number 62 and a half on Yidingpan Road in Puxi, a family surnamed Mou experienced a sudden burst in their water heater tube yesterday morning due to the water company's water supply being cut off without prior notice. A maidservant died on the spot. It was a tragic event.

The Citizens' Association's Stance

The Guowen News Agency reports: The Shanghai Special District Citizens' United Association sent a letter yesterday to the Shanghai Concession Taxpayers' Chinese Association, stating: Dear Sirs, Lately, the water fees calculated by meter in the concession are several times higher than the previous rates calculated based on house rent, with some even exceeding the rent. Landlords are unable to afford the increased costs when they are responsible for payment. Similarly, tenants (i.e., users) who pay directly are also unable to afford it. As a result, those who pay insist on paying according to the old system, while those who collect fees insist on collecting according to the new system. The subjective differences in sending and returning fees have made it impossible to resolve the issue. The Public Works Department, as the responsible party, must consider the interests of its constituents and the interests of the water company, seeking a legal, reasonable, practical, and feasible solution. However, the water company is impatient and, together with the police, has cut off the water pipes in Weishui Fang on Zhejiang Road and other areas, causing users to face the danger of being unable to cook or drink, a matter of life and death. If the Public Works Department fails to quickly stop this, it will inevitably raise suspicions of collusion with the water company. If both the payer and the collector of fees go to extremes and do not consider the difficulties faced by the third-party users and the agency responsible for maintaining the safety of residents' lives and property, the serious events that may result will be even worse than those caused by Director-General Lu He's oversight. This association believes that water is fundamentally different from telephones, electric lights, streetcars, tap water, and public buses. A lack of the latter does not lead to death, while a lack of the former makes survival impossible. Therefore, this is not a dispute between the water company and the tenants, but a dispute between those entrusted by the residents and the water company. If those entrusted disregard the interests of the residents and allow the water company to strangle them for money, the problem will become extremely serious. It has already evolved from a simple water fee issue into a highly complex issue of trust. Society will have its own judgment on whether the directors of the Public Works Department have made an effort to address the case. However, it is unwise not to correct the water company's recklessness and to allow it to wait for a resolution. This association believes that municipalizing the water supply would be a fundamental solution, while continuing to pay according to the old system would be a transitional measure. Based on the resolution of this association, we hereby request your association to authorize the Public Works Department to proceed quickly.

The Public Works Department Reconsiders

The Public Works Department Information Office announced that the Public Works Committee held a meeting several days ago to discuss the issue of installing water meters. During the meeting, the Director-General reported that, as a result of repeated consultations between representatives of the water company, Chinese groups, and personnel from the department, the water company had drafted a proposed alternative solution to reduce the burden on poor users under the meter system and eliminate opposition to the universal installation of water meters. After careful consideration by the committee, the report was presented to the Board of Directors on Wednesday of this week. The Board of Directors also discussed the matter in detail. Due to the need for careful study, no decision was made at that time. It was decided to reconsider and decide at the next meeting.

Chicago Centennial Progress Exposition

Opening This Afternoon

Chen Gongbo Presides Over the Opening Ceremony

Exhibition of Over 5,000 Items

The exhibition of items for the Republic of China's participation in the Chicago Centennial Progress Exposition has been in preparation for a long time and is now scheduled to officially open this afternoon. Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo will personally attend the opening ceremony. The exhibits from various regions, totaling more than 5,000 items, are exquisite, unparalleled, and valuable treasures, sufficient to represent our country's progress over the past century. The details are recorded below.

The Venue is Luxuriously Decorated

The venue for the exhibition is located at the newly built science and engineering hall of the Academia Sinica at 947 Bailinan Road, opposite Zhaofeng Park. All four floors of the building are used for the exhibition. However, the third floor is closed due to the unfinished construction of the building. A colorful archway is specially erected at the entrance of the venue, with the words ""Republic of China Exhibition for the Chicago Exposition"" written on a white cloth banner. The entrance is a passageway, and road signs direct visitors to the venue. The interior is decorated in an artistic and three-dimensional style, without using cabinets. It can be described as extremely luxurious.

The Opening Ceremony is Grand

The opening ceremony will be held at 2:00 PM this afternoon. The planned order is as follows: ㈠ All stand at attention. ㈡ Pay the highest respect to the Party's national flag and the portrait of the Prime Minister. ㈢ The Chairman respectfully reads the Prime Minister's will. ㈣ The Chairman delivers the opening speech. ㈤ The Preparatory Committee reports on the progress of the exhibition. ㈥ The Central Representative delivers a speech. ㈦ The Mayor delivers a speech. ㈧ Representatives of the Party and government organs in the city give speeches. ㈨ Guests give speeches. ㈩ Photography. ㈩㈠ The ceremony concludes. At the opening, the municipal government will send the Public Security Bureau band to play music. The Municipal Security Office will send a security team of 30 people to be responsible for protection. The Municipal Scout Council will send 50 male and female scouts to maintain order. The association issued more than 700 invitations to the ceremony yesterday. It is expected that there will be a lot of traffic and the event will be very lively.

Ladies and Celebrities Serve as Hosts

In addition to Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo serving as the chairman at the opening ceremony, Cai Wuji, the director of the exhibits department of the preparatory committee, is responsible for external affairs, while the internal affairs staff are divided into six sections: general affairs, display, storage, translation, communication, and entertainment. Each section has a director and several staff members. Xu Baohua is the director of the general affairs section, Miao Zhongxiu is the director of the display section, Yao Yinsheng is the director of the storage section, Zhu Yinong is the director of the translation section, Zhang Xianglin is the director of the communication section, and Wang Xiaolai is the director of the entertainment section. A exhibits review committee is also formed, and Cai Yuanpei is hired as the chairman, responsible for reviewing the exhibits to determine which ones to select and whether to transport them to the United States for competition. Ladies and celebrities, as well as the school flowers from various schools, are hired to handle the reception matters at the venue to ensure that everything is done well.

A Glimpse of the Exhibits - Over 5,000 Items

The exhibits collected for this exhibition are all valuable treasures, worth millions. The exhibits on the first floor include over 700 pieces of famous porcelain from Jiangxi, over 500 pieces of famous pottery from Yixing, lacquerware figures from Fuzhou, art health photography, famous fans from Hangzhou, Boshan glass, ivory carvings, Chinese and Western art, and various models from the Ministry of Railways, the city of Hangzhou, and the Thiepval Library, totaling more than 30 pieces. The second floor includes silk, tea, and agricultural products from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, new-style wooden furniture from Yilin, camphor wood furniture from Chai Songnan, embroidery and silk fabrics from Hunan, and self-woven silks from various factories. (There are no exhibits on the third floor.) The fourth floor contains various industrial products and sports equipment, including the Tai Chi equipment invented by Central Committee member Chu Minyi. In total, there are more than 5,000 items, which is enough to represent our country's progress over the past century.

Twenty-Four Postal Workers From the Suifenhe Area Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Subjected to Abuse by the Japanese When Leaving the Northeast

The Guowen News Agency reports: Our country's post offices in the three northeastern provinces were occupied by the puppet state. In July of last year, the Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang postal districts were successively closed to show resistance. At that time, the eastern part of Jilin (Suifenhe) and the Daheihe area of Heilongjiang were still occupied by righteous armies led by Ding, Li, Ma Zhanshan, and others, covering an area of over 700 li, with over 100,000 troops. Therefore, to facilitate communication for our righteous armies, our authorities decided to allow the 18 offices in the Suifenhe area and the 6 offices in the Daheihe area to continue operating as usual. The Ministry of Communications allocated several thousand dollars each month to provide assistance. The salaries for these two areas were paid until December of last year. Due to the repeated suppression of the righteous armies by the Japanese army, the postal workers in the two areas suffered greatly. As Ding, Li, Ma, and other units successively retreated to Russian territory, the remaining 24 offices could no longer continue to operate. They obeyed the order to withdraw. Some of the staff members risked taking the Chinese Eastern Railway and arrived in Shanghai one after another. However, the offices along the border, fearing interception by the Japanese, gathered in Vladivostok and took a route back to China. Those who arrived yesterday on the Russian ship "Lofsky" included Wang Zhongquan, the director of the Suifenhe office (with five family members), Zhang Sheng, the director of the Wuyun office (with two family members), Sun Shiyan, the director of the Chikht office, Zhang Chunxiang and Zhang Hengzhi, the assistant directors of the Daheihe office (each with two family members), and two messengers. There were also 13 people from the Suifenhe Customs and 3 staff members from the radio station. They said that they were subjected to abuse by the Japanese when leaving the country and were almost intercepted. Also, the remnants of Ding, Li, and Wang Delin's troops on the Chinese Eastern Railway line are still moving about unpredictably. When the war begins, many righteous armies in the three provinces will take the opportunity to rise up again.

Whether our opinion is appropriate, we ask the public to decide. Yours sincerely, Ge Zhaoqi, Guo Qiming, Gu Gongbing, Zhang Zanrong, Yan Dajue, Huang Yuping, Feng Buqing, Li Yiming, Liang Bohua, Wu Chengyu, Li Junhuan, and others.

Chu Minyi Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Gu Zhutong's Transfer to Gansu is Not True

Song Ziwen Will Return Soon

The Guowen News Agency reports: Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday. In the afternoon, reporters visited Chu at the Sino-French Institute of Technology and inquired about the Executive Yuan's recent affairs and Wang Jingwei's whereabouts. Their conversation went as follows:

Mr. Chu said that the Executive Yuan had not yet received Gu Zhutong's second written reply. The rumor that Gu had been transferred to Gansu and that Shao Lizi would be in charge of Jiangsu Province is not true. Mr. Shao is in Nanjing, and I have met with him. Although he has expressed his intention to resign, the central government still hopes that he will abandon this idea and return to his post soon. As for President Song, I called his residence and was told that he had not received a telegram. He will probably return soon. The mission of Mr. Song's trip has been reported in the Tianjin and Peiping newspapers for several days. One is related to finance, and the other is that Song is taking this opportunity to inspect the social conditions in North China. If Mr. Wang has left Lyon, he will likely arrive in Shanghai by the fifth or sixth of the next month. He will definitely take an Italian mail ship, as it is slightly faster than ships from other companies. The Executive Yuan has increased the navy's budget. As for the plan to develop the Northwest that I proposed earlier, the issue has been handed over to the National Economic Council by the Central Political Committee. In the future, we will probably need to convene a meeting of business leaders from the Northwest provinces in Nanjing and then discuss how to proceed. As for the Sino-Japanese issue, the rumor that Japan has issued an ultimatum to China on three fronts is completely false. Moreover, the central government has never received such a document. As for Japan's intention to withdraw from the League of Nations, this is probably just intimidation. However, in my personal opinion, if Japan can rein itself in at this time and end everything, even if it withdraws from the League of Nations, it may not be detrimental to Japan. If it continues to act arbitrarily, even if it does not withdraw, I fear that it will eventually offend the public and only Japan will suffer.

Chen Xunyong Transferred to Shanghai to Defend

Chen Jiliang Will Inspect Operations in Jiangyin

The Guomin News Agency reports that Chen Xunyong, commander of the naval training fleet, was originally in the capital in charge of defending the river surface. He has now been transferred to Shanghai by order of the ministry. He arrived in port yesterday morning at 11:00 AM on the Tongji warship and docked at the Gaochangmiao Wharf. In the afternoon, Mr. Chen went ashore to the naval headquarters to meet with Chen Jiliang, commander of the First Fleet. They had a long conversation and exchanged views. It is reported that Chen Jiliang will go to Jiangyin soon to command this year's naval spring exercises, while Chen Xunyong will be responsible for the defense of Shanghai.

Wireless Telegraphy Will Be Available Between China and England

China-Russia Wireless Telegraphy

International Wireless Telephone

The Ministry of Communications is also planning to do this

Wen Yuqing, director of the Bureau of International Telecommunications of the Ministry of Communications, told a reporter from the Central News Agency yesterday that the Ministry of Communications is actively working on wireless telegraphy between China and England. Five thousand pounds have been allocated and will be borrowed from the British Boxer Indemnity Fund. All the telecommunications equipment has been ordered from Marconi and is already en route. The location for the equipment has been decided: Zhenru. 250 acres of civilian land have been purchased for the construction of the building. Once the equipment arrives, it can be installed and telecommunications can begin. As for wireless telegraphy between China and Russia, such as international wireless telephone calls, the Ministry of Communications is also planning to do this and hopes to implement it in the near future. As for the cancellation of the MacKay Treaty, it is still in progress.

The British Lancashire Regiment Returns Home

They boarded the ship last night and set sail this morning

The First Battalion of the British East Lancashire Regiment stationed in Shanghai marched out of the racecourse barracks in formation at 1:00 PM yesterday to board the "New Laridia" transport ship. They are scheduled to set sail for England at 9:00 AM this morning. Before leaving the racecourse, Brigadier-General Fleming, the commander of the British forces stationed in Shanghai, addressed the entire team. The band of the Second Battalion, which had arrived in Shanghai from England a few days ago to replace the departing battalion, and the band of the Fourth Regiment of the U.S. Marine Corps stationed in Shanghai, escorted the team to the ship.

Party and Government Organs Mediate Huangpu Steamer Dispute Yesterday

New Voice Agency reports that the British Taikoo Company's expulsion of Wusong steamer workers has not been resolved. Recently, they intend to continue this method to deal with the Huangpu steamer, which has aroused the indignation of the workers on the steamer. They demanded the Chinese Cabin Public Office to find a way to stop it. Representatives of the Chinese Cabin submitted a petition to the Social Bureau yesterday. Party and government organs immediately sent personnel to mediate. The details are as follows:

Petition for Prevention: After receiving the request from the Huangpu steamer workers, the Chinese Cabin Public Office sent five representatives, Zhou Xiaoting, Qian Ziyun, Xu Yingsu, and others, to the Social Bureau at 11 am yesterday to petition for the prevention of disputes on the Huangpu steamer. Tan Peiyan, a mediator from the Third Section, received them and promised to report to the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Seamen's Special Party Headquarters to find ways to stop it.

Workers Confer: Representatives of the Chinese Cabin on various steamers of the Taikoo Company's Yangtze River route, and representatives of various cargo handling departments, considering that the Wusong case has not been resolved, and now the company intends to use this method to deal with the Huangpu steamer, then it is expected that this method will be gradually used to deal with other steamers. For the sake of their own interests, a joint discussion on countermeasures was held at the Chinese Cabin Public Office at 26 Jiuxiaochang Road in the city at 10 am yesterday. The result of the discussion was to unite and actively respond.

Party and Government Mediation: According to the request of the Chinese Cabin representatives, and because the Huangpu steamer will set sail tonight, the Municipal Party Headquarters dispatched Zhou Lianze, the chief of the Civil Training Section, the Social Bureau dispatched mediator Tan Peiyan, and the Seamen's Special Party Headquarters dispatched Xu Shiqi to mediate at 3 pm yesterday. According to the compradore Du Benchu, the company originally wanted to reduce the number of workers to twenty-three, but after negotiation, it agreed to reduce it to thirty. Party and government representatives then requested him to negotiate further, striving to employ as many workers as possible, and ordered the workers to board the ship and work first, and wait for a solution.

Strongly Opposing Water Price Increase

The Hongkou District Branch of the Citizens' Union (and the Jiaxing Road Wuzhou Road, Tangshan Road, Yangshupu Road, Yinxiang Road, Hambi Li Road, Haining Road, Dongyouheng Road, Zhaofeng Road, North Sichuan Road, Broadway Road, East Xihua Road, North Shanxi Road, Suzhou Road, Tangjialong, Aerjin Road, Jielu, and other business federations, more than 20 organizations in total), convened an emergency joint meeting at 2 pm yesterday. The resolution was to appoint Xing Guxiang and Zhang Xianfang to investigate and verify further. ㈤ The municipal house at the intersection of North Xizang Road and Haining Road was forced to increase rent by the owner. The resolution was to appoint Zhang Xianfang, Zhou Fuzhang, and Zheng Dongshan to handle the negotiation. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Representatives of Disaster Victims in Zhabei Disaster Area Petition for Relief

Sun Guixiang, Shen Musan, and other seven representatives of the victims in the Zhabei war zone, carrying petitions, went to the Municipal Government in Fenglinqiao at around 10 am yesterday to see Mayor Wu, requesting him to forward the petition to the War Zone Relief Committee for relief. Section staff Lin Yannan received them, and promised to forward the representatives' appeal and provide relief within the possible scope. The petition reads: "Submitted for the sake of disaster victims who are still displaced and have not had enough to eat, we hereby jointly and tearfully beg for relief. The representatives have petitioned repeatedly, and had no choice but to go to the government seven or eight times, appealing to the difficulties in person. We received three distributions of two or three liters of rice per person from Mr. Wang Binyan during the Lunar New Year, which shows the kindness to the disaster victims, and we benefited a lot. However, considering that each family has two people, how many people can be fed with such a small amount of rice, and how many people can survive? Although there is little porridge and many monks, the disaster victims are all singing praises. However, suffering frequently invades, and the spring is cold and the winter is harsh, and there is a shortage of food. The misery of water and fire is even deeper, and the tragic situation is unbearable to describe. The representatives hereby risk offending and submit this petition again, begging to distribute a small amount of relief money to each household to alleviate the suffering. We will be extremely grateful. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai War Zone Relief Committee."

Datongxing Yintai Bank Establishes Special Current Account Department

Yintai Bank, a member of the Ningbo Road Money Industry Association in this city, has been established for many years and has a good reputation. Recently, it has been observed that since the January 28th Incident, the industrial and commercial circles have suffered heavy losses. To revive the economy, it is necessary for the financial sector to cooperate fully. It is heard that after moving to its new location, the bank has established a special current account department to meet the above needs and changed the old practice of not opening current accounts without a street runner. At the same time, it has added time deposits. Regardless of the industry, anyone can open a current account with the bank without an introduction. The procedures are very simple. At this time of commercial decline, it is indeed good news for the industrial and commercial circles.

First Soviet Merchant Ship Arrives in Shanghai After Sino-Soviet Resumption of Diplomatic Relations

Flying the Chinese Flag Upon Entry

Carrying 66 Passengers

Since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union, the Soviet Union's business team has been recovering. Soviet merchant ships will first open the Shanghai-Vladivostok route. Although three chartered ships arrived in Shanghai last month, they were not regular ships of the team. Now, the team has specially dispatched the merchant ship Sharovsky for the first time, which sailed from Vladivostok to Shanghai. It was originally scheduled to enter the port on the afternoon of the 16th, but was delayed due to fog and changed to enter the port yesterday morning. When the ship arrived in Shanghai, it was inspected by the authorities as usual. The ship also flew the Chinese flag upon entry and sailed into the Huangpu River, stopping at the 92nd buoy. The ship is 375 feet long and has more than 2,000 tons. There are 66 passengers who came from Vladivostok, and hundreds of tons of cargo were loaded. It is verified that the ship is the first Soviet merchant ship to arrive in China after the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and the Soviet Union.

Press Figures Hold Farewell Dinner for Luo Fo Yesterday Evening

Luo Has Served as the Head of TASS in Shanghai for Six Years

His Successor, Cai Nash, Has Arrived in Shanghai

Luo Fo, the head of the Far East Branch of TASS, has served in China for six years. He has now been transferred back by the agency and will be appointed to an important position. His successor, Cai Nash, has already arrived in Shanghai. Luo Fo is about to leave. Zhang Zhuping, Dong Guangxian, Wang Yingbin, Pan Gongbi, Xiong Shaohao, and others from the Shanghai press hosted a farewell dinner for Luo at the Bank Club last night. Those invited included former Foreign Minister Chen Youren, Markhof, the head of the Russian Commercial Delegation Office who arrived in Shanghai three weeks ago, TASS Grass, Zhang Yunhe from Shen Bao, Wang Boqi and Wang Zhongwei from Xinwen Bao, Tang Liangli from Minzhong Luntan, Li Bingrui from Gonghe Zhoubao, Zeng Xubai from Da Wan Bao, Jiang Guangtang from Tianjin Yong Bao, and Zhang Si, the former Director of the Intelligence Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

Xu, etc., raised their glasses, talked and laughed, and the host and guests were extremely happy. Halfway through the banquet, Zhang Zhuping rose and delivered a speech, saying, "It is a great honor to have the distinguished guests here today. This is the first time that the Chinese and Russian press circles have gathered together after the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia. We have been wanting to have a good chat with you for a long time, but due to the busy newspaper work, we have neglected social contacts. Now that Mr. Luo Fo is about to return to his country, we have the opportunity to meet with you. We sincerely hope that those present tonight will expand the spirit of the joint celebration, so that the friendship between the two peoples will increase day by day, and we will support each other and develop business." After Zhang finished speaking, Luo Fo stood up and gave a reply in Russian, which was translated into English by Markhof, saying, "It is a great honor to be invited to participate in this grand banquet today. I wish to follow Mr. Zhang's words and congratulate the friendship between China and Russia on becoming closer and the development of business is promising. I also hope that after returning to China this time, I will have the opportunity to come to China again one day to continue the old friendship with everyone."

National Arts Circles Host Public Banquet for Ma Liang

Chairman Zhang Zhijiang's Welcome Speech

Zhang Zhijiang, Wang Ziping, Yu Zhongnan, Ma Zhongnan, Ma Haishan, and other representatives of the Central Guoshu Institute, totaling more than 70 people, held a public banquet at the Building at 24 Weihaiwei Road at noon yesterday for Ma Liang, the newly appointed General Counselor of the National Government. Tao Jianhua and others invited him to take a seat. Zhang Zhijiang was elected as the chairman and delivered a welcome speech, saying, "Our country is lagging behind others in everything, which has led to a weak country and poor people. Only Guoshu (National Arts) is becoming more and more prosperous. Recalling the end of the Qing Dynasty, all circles unanimously despised martial arts, but General Ma Zizhen, regardless of the opposition from all parties, shouted loudly and vigorously advocated it, which has led to today's achievements. General Ma has foresight and is worthy of admiration. Colleagues should follow General Ma and continue to work hard to popularize it among the 400 million compatriots, which is the foundation for a strong country. There is great hope," Next, Ma Liang gave a reply, saying, "The prevalence of Guoshu in the past ten years should be attributed to the enthusiasm and efforts of Director Zhang Zhijiang. I really dare not take the credit. I am very honored to be invited to this banquet by you all. I have three feelings. ㈠ The Japanese are pressing closer, which is unreasonable. I hope that compatriots will unanimously study Guoshu, every family will prepare a big knife, and everyone will prepare a walking stick to defend themselves, which is easy to do and can also prevent thieves. ㈡ Empty talk about promoting domestic goods cannot make up for the facts. Taking cigarettes as an example, most of the raw materials are foreign goods. The annual consumption is more than 98 million yuan. If this amount of money given to foreigners is used to run agriculture and industry, more than 9.8 million yuan of thieves, beggars, and vagrants can be reduced every year. In less than five years, the country will naturally become rich and strong. Therefore, everyone has the responsibility to save the country. ㈢ There are many Chinese and Western hospitals, pharmacies, and doctors in the country, but hospitals, pharmacies, and doctors for saving injuries are still rare. In this autumn of internal and external troubles, according to the proposal of Comrade Tao Jianhua, I have also had this idea for a long time and plan to actively carry out this matter. I hope that all circles will give guidance." Finally, 20 of Ma's subordinates performed various martial arts and dispersed.

Fujian Province's Exhibits for the Chicago Exposition Shipped to Shanghai

Since the Ministry of Industry's Preparatory Committee for the Chicago Exposition hired Mr. Dong Kunfan as the special commissioner for soliciting exhibits last September, the Fujian Preparatory Committee for the Chicago Exposition was established and began to solicit exhibits. Up to now, more than 4,000 exhibits have been received, including lacquerware, horn combs, paper umbrellas, tea, paper, porcelain, shiitake mushrooms, tobacco, silk, antiques, carvings, wood, bamboo, and other manufactured products and natural objects. Among the lacquerware, the products of the lacquer workshop of the Huieryuan Orphanage are the most distinctive, divided into three categories: ㈠ Improved daily necessities, that is, daily necessities for eating, drinking, sitting, and sleeping, and stationery, etc. In terms of materials, they are different from ordinary lacquer merchants. ㈡ Fine arts and crafts, such as Guanyin, Shouxian, Ruyi, coral, etc., and can also be lacquer models. ㈢ Among the cultural propaganda products, there are statues of ten famous people in ancient China, including the Yellow Emperor, Leizu, Confucius, Laozi, Wang Yangming, Yue Fei, Qi Jiguang, Lin Zexu, and Sun Yat-sen, all about two feet high. The above-mentioned famous people have made great contributions to the country and mankind. Now, the orphanage can make statues of their relics and promote national glory. This kind of work is truly commendable. It is verified that the orphanage was established in the spring of the eleventh year of the Republic of China (1922). At that time, the Minyue wars were raging, and natural and man-made disasters continued, and the social economy was completely bankrupt. Poor children were displaced. The founders of the orphanage, Mr. Shen Yonghao and Mr. Dong Kunfan, saw this situation and resolutely rose up to take on the task of saving the declining social economy. They jointly planned to establish educational institutions and began to organize the orphanage, running around and appealing, and operating in a difficult situation. After ten years of struggle and continuous efforts, there are now more than 180 students in the orphanage. The orphanage covers an area of 100 acres, including farms, forests, workshops (including lacquer, rattan, bamboo, sewing, and sericulture departments), classrooms, dormitories, libraries, etc., a total of more than 50 buildings. In addition, there are lacquer sales yards and trade departments. Dozens of students have graduated, and some talented children have been sent to major universities and specialized schools in China, as well as to naval and military academies, and have graduated and served the society. There are also more than 20 students studying outside the orphanage. It is verified that in the early days of the orphanage, the orphanage was narrow and the equipment was extremely simple. All the items in the orphanage were taken from the homes of the two gentlemen. It can be imagined that the two gentlemen worked hard to what extent at that time. This time, Mr. Dong served as the special commissioner for soliciting exhibits in the province. Because the matter concerns international honor, he is extremely enthusiastic. The first batch of items was personally brought to Shanghai by him and two graduates of the orphanage, Wang Hongci and Chen Chengzhang, a few days ago. They are now living in the Chicago Exposition Office, personally arranging the exhibits on the spot, day and night. This kind of enthusiastic and responsible spirit is truly a rare talent. As for the second batch of special products, it is heard that they will arrive in Shanghai soon.

A Tour of the Maritime Palace

Changxing Company's Civilian Empress of Britain

The First Giant Ship Imported After Shanghai's Opening to Trade

丨The Luxury and Splendor of the Ship Cannot Be Described丨

The world-cruising ship Empress of Britain, which was taken by the great British writer Shaw, arrived at Wusong at 6 am yesterday. The ship is Changxing's new ship and the first giant ship imported since Shanghai's opening to trade. Yesterday, the company invited people from all walks of life to visit the ship. The reporter also went to observe it. Its greatness and magnificence are truly the queen of the ocean. The situation is divided into the following:

Great Ship Body

Since Changxing Company built the 36,000-ton Empress of Japan in the Pacific Ocean the year before last, it has added the 42,500-ton net tonnage Empress of Britain in the Atlantic Ocean. The ship cost about 60 million yuan in Chinese currency, and the total displacement of the ship is 63,000 tons. It was launched on April 16 last year. The interior decoration took several months to complete. The machine is the latest style of diesel oil engine. Because of the great speed, it uses 60,000 horsepower and can travel 27 nautical miles per hour. There are three white painted chimneys on the body. There are 20 decks on the cabin, and there is an aircraft platform for adding when the voyage is official. The maiden voyage after completion is to travel the world and come to Shanghai. Because the ship is too large and eats too deep, it has to berth in Sanjiashui.

Rich Content

The layout of the ship's content is so rich and beautiful that it cannot be described in words. The great hall, smoking room, secondary room, etc. of the first-class room are in European style, with granite as the pillars, metal carvings, and the most valuable velvet carpets on the floor. The Chinese style is like the Swastika chair, all made of Quan wood and painted with Fuzhou's famous lacquer. There are countless ancient Chinese porcelain antiques, and there are also many famous paintings. The electric lights in each room use various kinds of hidden lamps, but emit light and do not see the lamps. The glass garden and dance hall are even more dazzling. The library, writing room, swimming pool, gym, tennis court, dining hall, etc. are far more luxurious than the major Pacific Ocean ships. People who enter it really have the feeling of being dazzled and brilliant.

Cordial Reception

This time, the ship's reception of visitors from all walks of life takes a strict approach. The company issued few invitations. At 2 pm, the Victoria ship was specially released to carry about 100 Chinese and foreign people who visited the ship. At 3:30, they arrived at the ship. The owner of the ship sent personnel to lead them to visit various places. The good management method of the whole ship shows the perfection of the travel settings, so that those who travel long distances have the joy of enjoying the scenery and no feeling of being isolated. At 4:30, the shipowner served tea and snacks to the guests. At 6 o'clock, they left the ship and returned to Shanghai by small steamer. It was already 8 pm when they arrived.

Tourist Itinerary

The 240 members of the world tour group who arrived in Shanghai by this ship were divided into Group A and Group B. Group A arrived in Shanghai at 9:30 AM, and Group B arrived at the port at 10:00 AM. Changxing hired 100 cars to guide them around the city. Group A toured the city and the Chinese area in the morning, while Group B visited the City God Temple and other places in the afternoon. By 5:00 PM, they all gathered at the Astor House Hotel. At 6:30 PM and 8:00 PM, they took the "Scott" and "Alexander" ships in two shifts to return to Wusong and board the big ship. However, because Mr. Shaw Desmond was welcomed by our side and time was limited, Changxing was asked to arrange a special small steamer at 10:00 PM at midnight to send Shaw on board. Therefore, the ship changed its departure time to 12:00 PM to leave Shanghai for Qinhuangdao.

Grand Lecture by Master Yuanying at the World Buddhist Laymen's Association

At the World Buddhist Laymen's Association on Xinmin Road, Zhabei, Venerable Yuanying, the executive director of the Chinese Buddhist Association, was respectfully invited to lecture on the Universal Gate Chapter of the Lotus Sutra Avalokiteśvara every afternoon at 2:00 PM from the 15th of this month, for a total of sixteen days. Although the spring rains were late and lingering, the gentlemen and ladies from all walks of life who went to listen to the lecture were extremely enthusiastic, so much so that there were no empty seats. The director of the association, Wang Yiting, the deputy director Wang Binyan, the directors Guan Jiongzhi, Li Jingwei, and the guests Wang Shaohu, Shen Binlun, and Yu Liaoweng all attended the association to listen respectfully. The master's voice was clear, and his analysis was detailed, and all the listeners were satisfied. It is expected that when the weather clears, the audience will be even more crowded.
