Shanghai Bank Safety Deposit Vault Adds Safety Deposit Boxes

Shanghai Bank on Ningbo Road originally had a safety deposit vault, equipped with more than 4,000 of the latest style safety deposit boxes. The vault is lined with half-hour thick steel plates on all sides, top and bottom, and the outer walls are up to eighteen inches thick. The vault door weighs fifteen tons. The construction is sturdy and unmatched in the country, and the rental fees are extremely low, so it was already fully rented out long ago. Those who came later often regretted being unable to secure a box. Last winter, the bank built a new safety deposit vault, with equipment identical to the original vault. At the same time, it purchased more than 2,000 safety deposit boxes from the United States. They have now been installed and are ready for use. The new boxes come in various sizes, and the rental fees start at four yuan. The number of people renting them has been very high in recent days.

Star Theater Donates to the Volunteer Army

The American-owned Star Theater on Qingdao Road, in view of the brave resistance of our Northeast soldiers against the enemy, showing boundless respect, but facing the isolated army fighting in a remote area, facing a powerful enemy advancing by land and air, with depleted ammunition and food, urgently needing supplies, the Shanghai Chinese movie theaters such as Central, etc. have already begun to voluntarily contribute. In order to take the lead in foreign movie theaters donating to the Northeast, the theater held a charity performance yesterday, donating all the proceeds from yesterday's ticket sales, as well as the shares of the staff, except for the film rental fees, totaling 113 yuan, to the Northeast Volunteer Army Relief Association, to do its part.

Reconciliation in Lawsuit of 111-Year-Old Li Fangxiao

The case of Li Fangxiao, a 111-year-old man, suing Feng Mingzheng, the manager of Foci Pharmaceutical Factory, for infringing on his reputation, was heard in the Fifth Division of the Shanghai Special Court at 2:00 PM on the 17th. The plaintiff's agent, lawyer Wu Kaisheng, and the defendant's agent, lawyer Yuan Jingtang, detailed the process of reconciliation between the plaintiff and defendant after the court's instructions. The judge advised both parties to be courteous, withdraw the lawsuit, and make peace, thus achieving reconciliation. As a result, the rare lawsuit between a 111-year-old man and a young man in his twenties came to an end.

A Retelling of the Multiple Robberies on Lunar New Year's Eve

One Robber Arrested and Shot Dead on the Spot

One Robber Injured, Interrogated Only Yesterday

On January 25th of this year, which was Lunar New Year's Eve, all the stores large and small in Shanghai were closing their accounts as usual, so those collecting debts were on the road all night long. A gang of robbers took advantage of this time to commit robberies. On that evening, from 7:30 PM to 8:15 PM, within those forty-five minutes, as many as four robberies occurred in the Beichengdu Road and Datong Road area of the Xinzha district alone. Not to mention other places, here is an exploration of the circumstances of the four robberies: The robber Deng Dahongzi, from Jiangbei, also known as Gao Xiaomao, specialized in forming gangs in Shanghai to commit illegal acts. He had been arrested multiple times but remained unrepentant. Recently, he became acquainted with Wang Zhaodi, a woman also from Jiangbei, and lived with her on Route Lafayette in the French Concession. Last Lunar New Year's Eve, Deng gathered his accomplices Jiang Weili, Shen Laosan, Dai Xiaohuaizi, Damao, and others to secretly plot a robbery. However, because carrying weapons was inconvenient, they entrusted his mistress Wang Zhaodi and Liu Dama to be responsible for transporting the weapons to avoid the attention of patrols. At 7:30 PM in the evening, the seven men and women set out together. When they reached the Chenjiabang vegetable market on Avenue Haig, Wang Zhaodi handed the guns and bullets to the group and waited near the alley entrance. Deng and the others first entered Wan Da Xin Sauce Garden at No. 377 Datong Road, took out their guns, and threatened them to be silent. They robbed eighty yuan in large and small silver coins from the counter and fled with the loot. They then went to the nearby Sen Tai He Cigarette and Paper Shop at No. 786-7, robbing 125 yuan in paper money. As they were fleeing, the shop assistant shouted "Catch the thieves!" The group fired three shots in the air to show their power and escaped. However, they were still not satisfied and went to Gu Changsheng Rice Shop at No. 617 Beichengdu Road, robbing 300 silver dollars, and then to the neighboring Tong Ren Cigarette and Paper Shop at No. 613, where an unfortunate incident occurred, otherwise, there may have been more than just these four cases. At that time, it was exactly 8:15 PM. There were many customers outside the counter of the store, and the shop assistants were too busy to attend to them. Suddenly, a thief jumped into the shop, took out his gun, and threatened them. He grabbed one hundred silver dollars from the drawer in the counter and jumped out of the counter with the loot, telling his accomplices who were on the lookout to flee south. Shen Zisheng, the shop owner, caught sight of him and quickly followed behind. Seeing the three thieves fleeing to Jing'an Temple Road and turning to Tongfu Road, Shen immediately reported to the Chinese policeman No. 3125 at the station, saying that the three people opposite were thieves and asking him to arrest them. However, the policeman felt that he was alone and afraid of alerting the snake, so he did not dare to take action rashly and also followed them secretly to observe their movements. After walking about 300 yards, a special Western policeman No. 83 happened to pass by. The Chinese policeman immediately informed him and asked him to arrest them together. Unexpectedly, the thieves were extremely alert and secretly noticed that there were police officers following behind. Deng Dahongzi immediately fled south, while the other two thieves fled north. The Chinese and Western policemen also chased after them separately. Chinese policeman No. 3125 closely pursued Deng but was unable to catch him for a while. Seeing that Deng seemed to want to resist arrest, he immediately raised his gun and fired five shots in a row. Deng fell to the ground in response. He was shot in a vital area and died instantly. The special Western policeman No. 83 turned to pursue the other two thieves, who also fired four shots in the air. Before long, the thieves disappeared. The policeman then helped the Chinese policeman to carry the thief's body to the mortuary for examination. When the Western policeman fired his gun, one of the thieves, Jiang Weili, was shot in the leg and fled in pain. That night, he returned to his home at No. 8 Yucheng Lane, Qiwupu Road, Yangshupu. Xu Bohua, who lived with him, telegraphed the Yulin Road police station in charge of the area, which sent detectives to arrest Jiang and transfer him to the Xinzha police station for questioning. Jiang also admitted to the robbery. The police chief, considering that his injuries were quite serious, sent him to the hospital for treatment. At the same time, he sent Chinese detective Ding Huaguo, Bao detective Zhou Jinshan, and Western detective Bai Naituo to investigate the case. On January 31st, Wang Zhaodi, the mistress of the deceased Deng Dahongzi, and Wang Xiaoerzi (i.e., Li Desheng), a suspect, were arrested at the Hongqiao in Xihua Road, Hongkou, and sent to the First Special Court for interrogation pending further questioning after Jiang recovered from his injuries. Jiang's injuries have now healed. Yesterday morning, the police sent Jiang and the two Wangs to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Special Court. The police summoned the victims of the robbery to court and presented the above situation in detail through police lawyer Wang Yaotang, stating that Wang Xiaoerzi was not related to the case and should be released first. After the trial, the police still need to request an extension because a robbery case had also occurred in the Yulin Road police station area. At that time, the thieves fired a gun. Afterwards, a shell was found and sent to the Public Works Department's Gun Inspection Office for verification. It was found to be the same as the bullet fired by the robber gang in the Sen Tai He robbery case on Datong Road.

Subsequently, representatives from each of the four victims arrived to testify about the robbery. Jiang Weili was questioned and claimed that he had sent vegetables to Deng's place in the afternoon, wanting to borrow money from him for the New Year. Deng told him to stay and go with him. At 7:00 PM in the evening, he followed the group out, but he did not know that they were going to commit a robbery. Wang Zhaodi testified that she carried three handguns for the thieves, from Route Lafayette to the Xiaocaichang vegetable market to commit the robbery. After the robbery, she still carried the handguns for them. Jiang Weili was indeed an accomplice at the time. After verification of the statements by Judge Qian Wenji, it was ordered that Wang Xiaoerzi be released first. Jiang Weili and Wang Zhaodi were detained pending further questioning on another date.

Wing On Company Wins Rent Lawsuit

Last winter, Wing On Company filed a lawsuit against Lang Jingji, a tenant of Minfeng Lane on Jiujiang Road, for prolonged rent arrears. The judgment was handed down, and the company appealed. The Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court has now ruled that Lang should repay six months of rent, totaling 450 taels of silver. The request for eviction was rejected because a public letter was sent by the Shanghai Municipal Government to the former Provisional Court in March of the 17th year of the Republic of China, stating that lease contracts of foreign merchants that do not specify a term should use the solar calendar. The lease contract between Wing On Company and Lang was established years ago and has always used the lunar calendar to record rent. Both parties should still be bound by it, so the respondent is ordered to pay rent according to the lunar calendar. Therefore, Wing On Company won the lawsuit.

Continued Hearing of Li Yushan's Case

Yin Geru Can Sue as a Shareholder

Yin Geru, a shareholder of Shashi Textile Co., Ltd., subscribed for 10,000 yuan of shares when the company was founded. He then mortgaged the shares to the Chongming Datong Bank for 3,000 yuan. At the end of last year, Yin decided to sell the shares. Through the introduction of Li Yushan, the general manager of Shashi Co., he sold them to Zhang Yunxuan, a tea merchant in Hankou, for the same price of 10,000 yuan. On the day of the transaction, Yin accompanied a friend to the Shashi Co.'s Shanghai office in Sanhe Lane, Jiangxi Road, to complete the transfer procedures. At that time, his shares had already been sent to the office by Datong Bank. Li ordered the accountant to pay over 3,000 yuan of Yin's mortgage principal and interest to Datong Bank. The remaining 6,000 yuan was given in Shanghai Bank promissory notes. After Yin accepted the promissory notes and handed them to his friend to take away, he suddenly asked Li to issue the dividends and interest for the three years since the yarn factory was established. Li believed that this was creating unnecessary problems and refused the request. Yin also refused to stamp the transfer seal on the shares. A conflict then occurred. Although Yin was reconciled by others and stamped the seal, he hired lawyer Ma Shouhua to file two criminal lawsuits against Li Yushan: (1) accusing Li and Yu Yingle of assault, and (2) accusing Li of embezzlement. The assault case has already been judged by the First Special District Court, sentencing Li and Yu to a fine of 50 yuan each. In the embezzlement case, Yin, as a shareholder, has filed four charges, which have also been heard twice by the First Special Court. Initially, there was hope for reconciliation, so only a brief hearing was held. Now, however, the path to reconciliation is full of thorns and impossible to proceed. Therefore, yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Tingqi reopened the trial. The defendant hired lawyers Qin Liankui and Xi Yafu to defend him. Judge Wu first rigorously examined the defendant's argument that the plaintiff's shares had already been sold, that the shareholder's rights had been lost, and that the shareholder's qualifications had naturally disappeared, so he had no right to sue. He then re-examined the facts of the conflict over dividends on the day of the transaction. After the plaintiff Yin Geru and the defendant Li Yushan each stated the situation on that day, Judge Wu believed that the shareholder's transfer procedures on that day had not been fully completed, so the plaintiff could still sue as a shareholder. He then ordered Yin Geru to state each of the four charges one by one. Yin then stated the facts of the first charge, saying that the defendant Li Yushan forged the name of Yan Deji (i.e., Dexiu) and embezzled 43,532 taels, one qian, and four fen from the company, which was obviously false. The defendant then answered this charge, and Li Yushan then stated that Yan Dexiu was also a shareholder of the company and a director. He was originally a shareholder and manager of the Tongxin Money Shop. Because Yan owed my Wanfeng firm over 43,000 taels of silver, and Shashi Co. owed Tongxin over 80,000 taels, Tongxin was affected by the current situation and stopped operating. Yan was unable to repay my debt at once, so I agreed with Du Shaoru, the chairman of Shashi Co., and other directors to transfer the account from Shashi Co. and noted under the name of Yan Deji that I would be responsible for this debt. If it could not be recovered in the future, I would still repay it. When the board of directors met in June last year, I reported it to the board of directors, and it was approved by all. The current board of directors met on February 10 and changed the name of Yan Deji to Li Yu Ji, with a fixed date for repayment. The above process was not only approved by the board of directors, but also ratified by the shareholders' meeting. The plaintiff's accusations are not true. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that the defendant embezzled over 40,000 taels of the company's funds. After the matter was discovered and questioned, it was only transferred to Yan Deji's name at the end of February of the 20th year. The board of directors' ratification was on June 22nd of the 21st year. Please pay attention to the timing. At this point, because it was necessary to summon witnesses, the trial was adjourned to February 27 for further hearing.

Indictment for Policeman Shooting and Killing Someone on False Charge of Robbery

Prosecutor Believes Policeman Disregarded Human Life

Jiang Boxian, a local from Xingju Lane, Nanhui Hall Road, organized a bidding club. Zhou Ronggui, a small owner of a Qinglong Bridge noodle shop, went to bid and won a round. Jiang thought that this round was paid for by Zhou's wife, so he asked for a guarantor. Zhou then gathered two hoodlums to coerce him and take the money away. Jiang's wife, Jiang Wu, went out and reported it to policeman Liu Sendong of the First District, First Precinct. Without asking the reason, he raised his gun and shot Zhou in the head, killing him. Now, after the review by the District Court Prosecutor's Office, the policeman is considered to have disregarded human life and violated Article 282 of the murder law. Jiang Boxian and Jiang Wu are accused of falsely accusing him of robbery. A public prosecution has been filed requesting a heavy sentence. The Criminal Division is currently reviewing the case.

Those who pass the review will be issued an exam certificate.

Those who do not pass the review will have their documents returned.

Shanghai Silk Industry Bank, located at No. 64 Hankou Road, is expanding its business and needs more staff than it currently has. Therefore, it plans to recruit trainees to assist in operations. Details have been published in previous newspapers. It is known that more than 250 male and female students have gone to the bank to register according to the registration procedures. Wu Chongjing's Boat Was Hit, Killing People. Request for Compensation

Xing Zhigang, a representative of the boat owners in Wu Chongjing, Pudong West, reported that the Ningbo ship and the Taiping ship collided, crushing Wu Chongjing's boat and killing many people on the spot. Yesterday, he sent letters to both companies and the Ship Inspection Department of the Customs, requesting compensation and condolences, stating that my people's boat is stationed in Wu Chongjing, Tangwan Town, Shanghai County, and travels back and forth to Shanghai every day, docking at the guild hall wharf in the southern city. Unexpectedly, at 11:30 AM on the 9th of this month, when the tide was rising, just as it was about to return to the countryside, it was suddenly hit by the Ningbo ship of Taikoo Company and the Taiping ship of Zhongwei Company, causing the boat to be turned sideways and crushed to pieces. Among the more than 20 passengers, some were crushed in the abdomen and drowned, including Sun Guanxi and Zhang Awu. Lu Weisheng was seriously injured, and there were still six or seven people who had not been recovered. Once the bodies and their families are identified, a supplementary report will be made requesting condolences. The people's boat is a boat that provides convenience to the countryside, transporting goods and passengers every day for a living. Now, it has suddenly suffered an accident. Not only were the boat and goods completely destroyed, with losses estimated at over 3,000 yuan, but many people were also injured and killed, leaving their families with no means of livelihood. In addition to waiting for the identification of the families of the victims and requesting to reserve condolences, the water patrol team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau has already investigated and recorded the case. A special document is prepared with a list of losses, hoping that the authorities will forward it, order prompt compensation, to benefit the boat owners and care for the lives of the people.

Northeast Students Staying in Peiping Will Run Out of Food

The Shanghai Charity Organizations Federation for the Relief of Northeast Refugees received a telegram from the Peiping Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang Relief Association yesterday, stating that the Northeast students staying in Peiping have set up a simple cafeteria. Director Qu had previously telegraphed to request assistance, and we are grateful for the donation of rice and flour, which has allowed the Northeast youth to survive. However, the two Northeast colleges, the Northeast University and the Northeast College, have a total of 1,262 Northeast refugees. Because it was easier to raise funds at that time, no cafeteria was established. However, since the tension in Yuyu, the donations have been few and far between, and the situation is becoming increasingly unsustainable and will soon run out of food. If relief is not considered, they will inevitably be displaced. After repeated negotiations with the simple cafeteria, it has been said that they are unable to cope. Considering the situation, it is necessary to provide relief to the Northeast refugees in the same way to prevent them from having nowhere to turn and becoming starving corpses. It is estimated that about 5,000 yuan of rice and flour expenses are needed per month, calculated for six months, totaling 30,000 yuan. Graduates in the summer vacation will be provided with other arrangements, and further assistance will be sought for those who continue their studies. Current relief efforts cannot be delayed. We dare to state the difficult situation and respectfully ask the comrades of the congress to propose and fully support the cause. We hope that it will not be regarded as an ordinary fund-raising effort, which is what we urgently hope for. We also hope to receive a reply.

Resolution of Labor Dispute at Da Jin Silk Factory

Each person receives a severance payment of 95 yuan.

Injured receive medical expenses of 250 yuan.

After the entire workforce of the Da Jin Silk Factory on Xietu Road, Nanshi, had a dispute over the dismissal of workers, personnel were dispatched by party and government agencies to mediate. Yesterday, labor and management reached a resolution in consultation with the city party headquarters. The agreement is recorded as follows: At 10:00 AM on February 17th, 22nd year of the Republic of China, Hou Xuecheng and other workers of Da Jin Silk Factory resolved the labor dispute with the company in the city party headquarters as follows: (1) Hou Xuecheng, Ma Ruxian, Ma Shanhai, Ma Yaohai, Zhang Nancheng, Zhao Xingen, Xu Zuyuan, Xu Zuyao, Wu Aquan, Ma Fuquan, and other ten people are allowed to be dismissed by the factory, and each person will receive a severance payment of 95 yuan from the factory. (2) In addition to the above severance payment, Ma Fuquan will also receive a medical expense allowance of 250 yuan from the factory. (3) Hou Xuecheng and others shall publish an apology to factory director Yang Zhenliang in the newspaper. The above three items have been agreed upon by both parties, and the record of settlement has been signed on the spot as above. Witnesses: Zhu Guilin, Zhang Dafu.

Weiting Central Elementary School Initiates the "Wu County Children's Aircraft"

Last year, all teachers and students of Weiting Central Elementary School enthusiastically supported the Northeast Volunteer Army. In total, over four months (starting from October), the children and teachers saved their daily allowances and collected a total of more than forty yuan. The school principal already remitted this amount to the Shanghai Volunteer Army Support Association for transfer to the Northeast. Although this year's winter vacation was short, the children of the school, realizing that the work of national salvation cannot be interrupted, decided to donate all of their Lunar New Year lucky money and candy expenses during the vacation. According to recent statistics, the amount obtained is over twenty-five thousand yuan. After collective discussion, it was decided to temporarily conclude the efforts to aid the Volunteer Army. Starting in February of this year, all children in the school will voluntarily save money daily, and teachers will contribute one percent of their salaries to initiate the fundraising to purchase a "Wu County Children's Aircraft" bomber for national air defense. However, because this is a major decision, a circular will first be sent to all elementary schools in Wu County to proceed uniformly, and a request will be submitted to the Wu County Party Headquarters, Party Government, Education Bureau, and Education Association to request leadership and organization to complete this endeavor as soon as possible under unified command.

Fujian Education Department Improves Middle School Standards

Dividing into Two Methods: Addressing the Root Cause and Treating the Symptoms

Recently, in order to improve the standards of middle school students, the Fujian Education Department divided into two methods, addressing the root cause and treating the symptoms, to actively improve the situation. ⑴ Addressing the root cause: Starting from this semester, urge all middle schools to rectify the academic atmosphere, strictly enforce training, improve teaching, and expand equipment to ensure that middle school education cultivates the backbone of the Chinese nation. ⑵ Treating the symptoms: ⑴ Organize a textbook research committee for primary and secondary schools: In order to improve the efficiency of primary and secondary school teaching, this committee is specially organized to guide the adoption of textbooks in primary and secondary schools in the province based on the curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education, and to investigate and review textbooks and supplementary teaching materials for various subjects. ⑵ Improvement of the unified examination method: According to the unified examination questions in previous years, the standards were based solely on the school graduation course. This method has caused many malpractices. It is now changed to formulate test questions based on the middle school curriculum standards promulgated by the Ministry of Education and the subjects taught over three years. ⑶ Formulate regulations for unified examinations for normal schools and vocational middle schools: In the past, unified examinations were limited to ordinary middle schools, and normal and vocational schools were not included. Even the Ministry of Education did not set unified examination rules for these types of schools. Director Zheng believes this is also necessary, and it is said that detailed rules are being drafted. ⑷ Plan to set up college preparatory classes: In order to remedy the academic level of previous graduates, college preparatory classes will be held in the provincial capital. It is said that the regulations have been drafted and submitted to the provincial government for approval.

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Pays Attention to Health Education

Instructions on Matters Requiring Attention from Various Schools

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued the following instructions yesterday to schools below the secondary level in the city: It is found that all faculty and staff should be responsible for health education in schools. For the sake of convenience, physical education teachers in each school should be responsible for guiding and planning physical education in the entire school. The director of general affairs and the director of student affairs should pay more attention to school hygiene matters. When hygiene workers come to the school, they must sincerely assist in handling matters. In smaller schools, the principal and class teachers should also provide appropriate assistance to facilitate progress. In addition, various health records of students are as important as other school documents and should be properly preserved to prevent loss for future reference and investigation. These orders must be followed. This order.

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Requests Early Promulgation of "Children's Day Song"

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau submitted a request to the Ministry of Education yesterday for the early promulgation of the "Children's Day Song" and a clear order stipulating that schools be closed for one day on Children's Day, stating: In March of last year, this bureau submitted a request to your ministry to create a "Children's Day Song" and issue it to the whole country for singing. We received your ministry's instruction No. 3159, stating that the submission was noted and that the song had been collected by various departments. However, as this year's Children's Day is approaching, it is too late to issue the song, and the Party song can be used temporarily at that time, and we were instructed to comply. We have already complied with these instructions. This year's Children's Day is approaching in a flash. If this song has been created, we request that it be issued as soon as possible so that we can instruct rehearsals. Also, there are no clear regulations regarding whether schools should be closed on Children's Day. According to the facts, it is difficult to have classes on that day. May we request that your ministry inform all primary schools and kindergartens throughout the country to close for one day on Children's Day to hold various activities in order to unify the practice. We have submitted this document for your review and instruction.

Baoshan Education Funding Granted Exemption from 10% Discount

Since the Baoshan County education funding was affected by the January 28th Shanghai Incident, income has sharply decreased. Therefore, a 10% discount was applied to the funding for bureaus, schools, fields, and museums. Subsequently, Director Feng of the Education Bureau repeatedly explained the difficult situation to the Education Department and requested permission to waive the discount. Now, the Education Department has issued instructions for approval, so the bureau has issued notices to various schools. The original order is recorded as follows: It is found that since the bureau, schools, fields, museums, and other expenses have been issued at a 10% discount, the situation has been extremely difficult. We requested that the discount be waived starting from the second half of the year. Now, we have received the Education Department's instruction No. 720, stating that the submission has been noted. It is verified that the difficulties described are indeed factual. However, there is a need to reduce revenue after the disaster and to make special reductions in expenditures. If we only take care of the present and do not consider the future, the difficulties will be greater than today when unforeseen circumstances arise. Since repeated requests have been made to waive the 10% discount, permission is granted to temporarily waive the discount from the second half of the 21st year, but all temporary expenditures should still be greatly reduced. This order must be complied with. This order.

Municipal Education Bureau Promulgates Rules for the Review Committee for Opera Records

The rules of the Opera Record Review Committee of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau have been submitted by the bureau to the municipal government for approval and record. The rules are recorded as follows: Article 1: This committee is organized by the director of the bureau in accordance with Article 10 of the bureau's rules for reviewing opera records. Article 2: This committee shall have twelve to fifteen members, and the chairman shall be appointed by the director of the bureau. Article 3: This committee shall handle the following matters under the direction of the director of the bureau: 1. Review and supervise various opera records performed and produced in this city. 2. Issue performance and sales licenses. 3. Commend excellent opera records. 4. Ban substandard opera records. 5. Deliberate on violations. The execution of the above items shall be implemented after being resolved by this committee and approved by the director of the bureau. Article 4: This committee may set up various sections, such as opera, lyrics, music, miscellaneous plays, song and dance records, etc., to handle the various matters in the preceding article separately. Article 5: This committee shall hold a regular meeting once a week, and special meetings may be convened when necessary. Article 6: Matters not covered by these rules may be amended at any time. Article 7: These rules shall be implemented after being approved by the bureau affairs meeting and submitted to the municipal government for record.

As long as they have the appropriate qualifications and are recommended by public organizations, they can enroll. The application period is limited to the end of February.

Unified Examination Series Actively Adopted by Various Schools

Reservations Close Soon

Since the news of poor unified examination results in Shandong, Nanjing, Zhejiang and other places has spread to Shanghai, all schools have been learning from the past and preparing for the future, and have been ordering the middle school and elementary school unified examination guidance series published by the publishing department of the Datong Bookstore and Chenbao News Agency. A total of more than 800 sets have been sold in one week. It is reported that many schools have adopted this series of books as teaching materials for reviewing various subjects. Publication of the Theory and Practice of the Central Primary School District System

In recent years, the central primary school district system has been implemented in various places, and everyone is suffering from the lack of specialized books for reference. Jiading County, Jiangsu Province, was the earliest to implement this system, and it was handled perfectly with remarkable results. Now, Yang Baohe and Zhang Naixuan of Jiading have combined their experience and insights to compile the book "The Theory and Practice of the Central Primary School District System." The entire book has 16 chapters, and the motivation, organizational principles, implementation methods, and results are written out one by one. The preface has prefaces by Wu Yan, Yin Cheng Shichui, and Yang Naikang, and the end of the article includes criticisms and opinions from educators. It is the only specialized book after the implementation of the central primary school district system and can be used as a reference for colleagues serving in the education field. The actual price is nine jiao. It is available at the Jiading Education Bureau, Shanghai Life Bookstore, Great Wall Bookstore, and major bookstores in this city and other cities.

Seven Hours of Classes Per Day

Appointment of staff of this committee (Resolution) First, two staff members will be dispatched by the Ministry of Education to serve concurrently. If the affairs become complicated, the increase will be considered. 3. Draft the detailed rules of this committee (Resolution) The detailed rules will be drafted by the Social Affairs Department in consultation with the Department of Physical Education of Central University and submitted to the next meeting for discussion. 4. Ding Class Director and Faculty (Resolution) It will be submitted for discussion next time. 5. Curriculum (Resolution) ⑴ Those who pass the examination will be issued certificates by the Ministry of Education with the subjects passed listed, but no credits will be given. ⑵ After the examination is over, the recommending organizations should be notified for verification. ⑶ Class time is from 7:00 AM to 11:00 AM and from 4:00 PM to 7:00 PM, a total of 7 hours per day, 4 hours of academic subjects, 2 hours of practical subjects, and 1 hour of lectures or discussions. ⑷ The proposed curriculum will be amended and passed, and then printed for submission to the next meeting for careful discussion. The content of the curriculum includes 6 required academic subjects, 14 hours per week, 11 elective subjects, 10 hours per week for elective subjects, and practical subjects are divided into 5 groups for national defense and 5 groups for ball games. In addition, there are various types of field games, dances, swimming, etc.) 6. Student Meals and Accommodation (Resolution) All students will live in Central University and take care of their own meals (this class will designate a kitchen to handle it). 7. Date of the next meeting (Resolution) Next Wednesday (the 22nd of this month) at 5:00 PM, the meeting will be held and adjourned at 8:00 PM. Page 17

Spring and Autumn on George Bernard Shaw by Fei Ming

{Use the laughter that comes with tears to satirize this great writer}

Among the world’s great writers whose names have been translated into Chinese and are well known to Chinese people, Maxim Gorky and George Bernard Shaw are probably the most famous.

BernarShaw is not translated as “Berna Shaw,” but rather as “George Bernard Shaw.” Some people think it’s because the translator is too familiar with the Chinese surname book, but in fact, it’s better to say that it’s the translator’s painstaking effort. First, “George Bernard Shaw” is smoother to read than “Berna Shaw.” Second, this great writer is a satirist with a strong Chinese flavor. Apart from his accent, clothing, and diet, his words and deeds are not like those of a mechanized European, but rather like a caricatured Oriental. The translation of “George Bernard Shaw” is a symbol of this old gentleman’s life and personality being close to the Oriental flavor.

Now, the great writer we admire has come to China from afar. What he brings is not opium guns and cannons to poison us, but rather a profound sense of humor that resists the darkness of the present. What should we, who are impoverished, offer to him, the old gentleman? I think there is nothing else but the boundless laughter that comes with tears surrounding him!

Yes, George Bernard Shaw is a humorous socialist. In order to guess the mysterious secrets of socialism, he once visited the Soviet Union regardless of everything. His relatives and friends, fearing that he would be starved and frozen to death by the "red demons," prepared a large amount of bread and luggage for him, but he refused these gifts and finally entered another new world from the flood of panic. Amidst the grand welcoming sound, the great writer witnessed everything and suddenly realized that boring slander and rumors were enough to block the wisdom of the world. So after he returned home, he wrote down his impressions of the Soviet Union as they were.

China is a pitiful nation that has been living in the wanton insults and slanders of invading robbers. "Barbarian nation" and "uncivilized country" are the infamous names that all imperialists have given us. Now, our great writer wants to visit China regardless of everything to see what kind of nation China is and what kind of deeds the so-called "civilized people" are doing in China.

Unfortunately, when Mr. George Bernard Shaw and his wife came to Shanghai, it was the early spring when the winter cold had just receded. If it were in the autumn when ten thousand trees shed their leaves, we could use a Tang poem to welcome them:

The boundless falling leaves rustle down, the endless Yangtze River rolls on! (Note) Note: In that deep autumn when ten thousand trees shed their leaves without end, our Mr. Shaw and Mrs. Shaw stepped off the English Queen’s ship with smiles and stepped onto the territory of China, while the rolling Yangtze River corresponded with the grand laughter of the welcomers?

Flying Tour of the Great Wall by Hui Zhu

{“Flying Tour of the Great Wall” is such a magnificent and joyful thing!}

George Bernard Shaw once said before leaving England: "After arriving in China, I will take a flying tour of the Great Wall."

But it was beyond expectation! On January 3rd, Yuguan fell and the Guanshan Mountains were lost! The world’s first pass, the great and magnificent symbol of Eastern history and culture that I yearned for, and the plaque of the first pass, have already been sent to Tokyo for display!

“Things go contrary to wishes!” So extremely disappointed! I dare not have such extravagant thoughts anymore!

The reality is far beyond expectation! Shenyang fell in one night, and Jinzhou was defeated in one month. Yuguan fell, and Pingjin was already in danger! Or, due to "strategic considerations," they will retreat to the south of the Yellow River!

But since I have arrived in the Orient, there is always a glimmer of hope. "I don’t want the war in North China to stop me from traveling.” Let’s just take a trip to Beiping and admire the cultural city of the East!

The public banquets and welcomes all seem to be the conditions for exchanging speeches.

"I will repay you with a tour of the Great Wall." So extremely clever, they hit his sweet spot. It's just a pity that these words were said at the wrong time. The Japanese have clearly occupied Shanhaiguan! At Jiukou, there is still a part of the loyal Yong soldiers sacrificing their lives! Although it is said that the Great Wall is called the Great Wall of Ten Thousand Miles, there is no need to care about a corner of Yuguan!

Zhang Eyun's Success by Plum Blossom Hall Master

{Comes from the four words "determined ambition"}

Zhang Eyun is a person who is not destined to be with old operas. Since the age of eleven or twelve, she has been immersed in the singing stage and dance pavilion almost every day, and constantly works hard while studying other people's strategies and tactics. It is rare to be so obsessed with opera like this lady. During this process, she once became a concubine of a wealthy family. Although life was very comfortable, she felt that it was not in line with her interests because she could not learn and sing opera every day. As a result, she was willing to leave the wealthy family with rich clothes and fine food and continue her wandering life as an actress. Her perseverance and determination are truly admirable. Zhang Eyun has repeatedly said to people: "I have been obsessed with opera for more than ten years. If I don't perform on stage in Shanghai once, I will never stop my efforts and struggles." Now she has actually achieved her goal, and the reputation she has gained is also very good. The ancients have a saying, "Where there is a will, there is a way." Zhang Eyun's success definitely comes from the four words "determined ambition." It can be seen that when a person does things, no matter how big or small, noble or lowly, as long as they are willing to set a goal and be determined to do it, there is no reason for it not to succeed.

Novel The Fire of Youth by Gu Mingdao

One evening, Kaijun and his mother had just fallen asleep when they suddenly heard a faint sobbing sound coming intermittently. Listening to it,

Work Plan Compiled by the Wharf Affairs Office

Since its establishment, the Shanghai Municipal Wharf Affairs Office has been working extremely intensely. It has now formulated a work plan that includes the following eight major items: 1. Work Outline, 2. Work Procedures, 3. Preliminary Investigation, 4. Training of Cadres and Workers, 5. Second Stage Investigation, 6. Registration Work, 7. Guidance and Organization of Labor Unions, and 8. Improvement of Workers' Living Conditions. The Work Outline is further divided into A. Principles: (1) Handling matters between labor and contractors, (2) Guiding the organization of genuine worker labor unions that are beneficial to workers, (3) Improving workers' living conditions; and B. Steps: (1) Investigation: Investigating relevant facts as the basis for plans, guidance, labor union organization, and plans to improve workers' living conditions. (2) Planning: Based on the investigation results, considering factual needs to plan implementation schemes. (3) Implementation: Properly implementing plans and schemes. (4) Transfer: After the amendment and promulgation of the Labor Union Law, formally establish labor unions, and all labor union-related affairs should be transferred to the labor unions for self-management. The office is currently actively carrying out its work according to the plan, which is truly good news for the 80,000 dockworkers in this city. (Details of work procedures, etc., are omitted due to length).

The Effectiveness of Bingxun Chinese Shorthand

Boy Hong Ronghua Waiting to Be Claimed

Reader Advisory

How to Strive?

丨Letter from Mr. Chen丨

After reading your reply to Mr. Ren Yuewang the other day (regarding suicide), I still have some questions. I dare to ask for your further guidance, as I also harbor the thought of "suicide" from time to time.

I am an apprentice in a shop, living the life of a slave all day long. (I don't know how to describe this painful situation, but it is extremely painful!) Besides "suicide," what other options are there? (I also know about striving, but I don't know how to strive. Once I wage war against the forces of darkness, I immediately face the risk of unemployment, which means the risk of hunger and cold.)

Since you said that "suicide" is the shameful mentality of a coward, and that one should strive and wage war against the dark society, I wonder if you could tell us "how to fight."

Answer: Although your letter is very simple, the questions you ask are very reasonable. I will answer in general terms as follows: (1) Apprentices who want to improve their lives (as is the case with all workers) must get rid of an old concept, namely, the old concept of thinking only from the perspective of oneself or one's own interests. The current society is often in a state of opposition between one group and another. The reason why shopkeepers dare to mistreat apprentices is one manifestation of this state. For the present, apprentices should unite everyone's strength to seek happiness for the entire common people in society, and at the same time seek to improve the lives of shop assistants or apprentices themselves, and make various reasonable demands on the shopkeepers. We know that young shop assistants not only feel the hardship of material life, but also feel the urgent need to satisfy their spiritual life and cultural life, and their desire for knowledge. Apprentices should find ways to carry out this educational work themselves. If this is achieved, then there is other striving to speak of. If everyone only thinks of themselves, perhaps you will have the opportunity to escape the position of shop assistant or apprentice and climb to the position of shop owner. This is another question, which the reporter does not want to hear, nor dare to know.

Free Talk Shaw Corner (Continued)

On Shaw

— Xuan

In his essay "Quintessence of Ibsenism," Shaw discusses Ibsen, saying: "People blindly adhere to some incorrect ideas (regarding religion, politics, and gender relations) and allow these ideas to control their actions, even though they are unwilling in their hearts; and Ibsen's satire is aimed at this contradictory state."

We believe that Shaw is similar to Ibsen in this regard. Shaw's important works all expose the errors in people's traditional concepts (and these erroneous concepts are maintained by the rulers through various means). However, Shaw is more profound than Ibsen. For example, regarding the traditional and erroneous concept of "duty," Shaw says: "Civilized people often use the term 'duty' to disguise the true face of their actions." In the play "The Man of Destiny," Shaw uses Napoleon's mouth to say: "The English always have to come up with some grand principle to justify their actions. If he wants something in his heart, he will never say what he wants... When he wants to find a new market for the manufactured goods of Manchester, he first sends out some pastors to preach the gospel of peace. But if the natives harm the pastors, the English immediately jump up and take up arms to protect Christianity; they wage war and conquer for Christianity, and thank God for the gift of occupying that new market." In plays such as "Candida" and "Widower's Houses," Shaw mocks those hypocrites who have "fulfilling obligations" on their lips but are always thinking of their own selfish interests, truly striking with every word.

In "The Man of Destiny," which features Napoleon as the protagonist, and "Caesar and Cleopatra," which features the Roman general Caesar as the protagonist, Shaw mocks the world's "hero worship." In Shaw's pen, the "hero" is a very foolish and selfish person.

At the same time, these two historical plays are also "anti-war." However, Shaw's "anti-war" plays should be primarily "Arms and the Man" and "Major Barbara." The former exposes the psychology of soldiers in commercial countries towards war: "It's fear of death that makes them fight!" The latter exposes that not only are machine guns, torpedoes, and other weapons of destruction lethal weapons, but also fine-sounding terms such as "patriotism," "religion," "justice," and "duty" are also lethal weapons.

Many people believe that the play "Man and Superman" contains Shaw's "philosophy," so its value is above other plays. Indeed, "Man and Superman" not only mocks the world's views on love, but also puts forward a "philosophy": "We humans are just an experimental product, a link between beast and superman, and love is just a means for nature to achieve its purpose (to superman)." Love is a great "Cosmic Force." Shaw wrote tens of thousands of words in the preface to "Man and Superman" to explain his philosophy. People who like to study love as a "philosophy" can read that play and that long preface. But don't be too happy. Because if you read "Man and Superman" twice, you will learn that Shaw may be laughing at those "love philosophers" there.

Since the May Fourth Movement, Shaw's name has been frequently mentioned in our literary world. Several of Shaw's works have also been translated into Chinese. However, there is still very little research on Shaw. Taking advantage of this moment, if we seriously study Shaw, it may not be a bad thing.

The Story of the Black Woman Seeking God (4)

— Written by Shaw, Translated by Yi Xian

"Good!" said the god. "This is exactly what I want you to ask me. You are a clever and knowledgeable woman. I used to argue with a servant of mine named Job; but he was truly old and truly foolish, and I had to pour the most terrible disasters upon him before I could provoke him to complain. His wife taught him to curse me and then die; I don't blame the poor woman, because I did give him terrible light after all, although I later fully compensated him. When I finally got him to argue, he became presumptuous. However, I immediately exposed his true nature. He admitted that I was superior to him. I skillfully subdued him, I tell you honestly." "I don't want to argue," said the black girl. "I want to know: if you really created this world, why did you make it so bad?"

"Bad?" said the skillful one. "Oh! Are you standing up to teach me to explain myself! May I ask who you are! You can criticize me? Could you create a better world yourself? Try it: that's all there is to it. Try creating a little bit of it. For example, make a whale. Once you've made it, stick an iron hook in its nose and bring it to me. You ridiculous little insect, do you understand: I not only made the whale, but also the ocean for it to swim in, that ocean, down to the bottomless depths, up to the top of the sky. You think it's easy, I guess. You think you could do this better yourself. Girl, listen to me; you have to get rid of your conceit. You can't even make a mouse, yet you stand up against me, the maker of the great sloth. You can't even make a pond, yet you dare to chat with me, the creator of the seven seas. In fifty years you will become ugly, old, and die, while my majesty will continue forever; now you are criticizing me as if you were my aunt. You think you are better than God, don't you? What do you have to say about this debate?"

The Bees of the Gentleman Class

— Xu Jie

Shaw is a bee in British gentleman society; he has a sting, and he can also make honey; however, the honey he makes is sweet with a touch of sourness.

There is more than one British gentleman; therefore, when this bee relentlessly stings one gentleman, the other gentlemen think that it has not stung them, so they laugh; at the same time, the gentleman who is laughed at by others for being stung by a bee also discovers that the few gentlemen who laughed at him have been stung by this annoying bee, so he also laughs.

But in British society, in addition to a large number of gentlemen, there are also many people who are not qualified to be included in the ranks of gentlemen. In their eyes, these gentlemen all seem to suffer from cleanliness; their formal wear is perfectly tailored, the collar, cuffs, and chest are all ironed perfectly: white collars, white cuffs, white shirts. They are not happy to even use two fingers to pick up a little bit of dirty stuff. What an unbearable thing this is! Now, they are seeing with their own eyes that this bee is buzzing into the gentlemen's collars, cuffs, and chests to sting them, making these gentlemen helpless, making them perform many laughable strange plays; therefore, these people who are not in the gentleman class are also watching and laughing.

This is probably what makes Shaw Shaw.

Shaw's Drama

— Translated by Zhao Liang Shen

Manly and Rickert

The change in British drama is undoubtedly due to Ibsen. Ibsen was introduced very early in the 1870s by Gosse (Edmund Gosse). Between 1872 and 1880, Archer (William Archer) and others translated some of his plays; in 1880 his play, a translation or adaptation of A Doll's House, was staged and performed twice a week between 1880 and 1890. In 1890 and 1891, five of his plays were regularly performed. The most notable of these five plays was Ghosts, as it was the opening play of the Independent Theatre's inauguration ceremony (on March 13, 1891). For six years, this theatre struggled for the sole purpose of presenting new dramatic forms to the public. This theatre was able to develop entirely thanks to the ambition and courage of a Dutchman, Grein (J. T. Grein).

Shaw was initially an admirer of Ibsen, and he was the first person in England to use the Norwegian method as the starting point for a new British drama. The performance of his Widowers' Houses (1892) was a powerful start to the new movement. To understand that Widowers' Houses completely removed the old materials and techniques, the following summary must be known:

(1) The characters in the play are all middle class.

(2) Love is not important; the problem is the evil of landlordism.

(3) The structure does not conform to any known plan.

(4) Discussion replaces mechanical structure.

(5) No distinction is made between the structure and the evenness of the characters.

(6) The characters are not traditional representatives, but merely spokespersons for Mr. Shaw's views on economic issues.

(7) Elaborate sets and short scenes are obviously absent.

(8) Traditional stagecraft is obviously absent.

(9) Emotionally stirring eloquence is replaced by debate.

(10) Limestone lighting is replaced by ordinary setups in ordinary people's normal lives.

From this beginning, Shaw made somewhat systematic attacks, using drama as a weapon to attack many great thinkers of his time, and also somewhat systematically promoted himself. He deliberately chose his attacks, often changing them to avoid repetition. Reading all of his plays over the years, one can reconstruct his developed social philosophy and his propaganda for social reform.

Speaking of literature, Shaw's dramas, in addition to breaking away from early dramatic traditions, also have other aspects; the organization of these dramas has the following four points:

(1) Regarding the social purpose of these dramas, they should not only be performed, but also be read; not only read, but also understood. Therefore, attention must be paid to Shaw's famous prefaces, some of which are indeed longer than the plays themselves, and are still just as interesting.

(2) Because these dramas are intended for reading, the stage directions should be developed to stimulate the reader's imagination, constructing for themselves what their eyes cannot see; therefore, the use of narrative and description in stage directions should be promoted to the point of becoming a new literary form: the "Closet" drama.

(3) Without the self-recitation and climaxes of past emotions, nor the old method of dividing into acts; the drama can be divided into as many acts as needed, as long as it is not too long and does not tire the audience's attention.

(4) To reduce physical movement on stage, in addition to the well-known and always clichéd drawing rooms and garden scenes, there should also be a focal point of vision. Therefore, new and even strange sets and props have been invented: for example, the car used in Man and Superman in 1901; you can never say that the dentist's office used in the play is ordinary.

The current effect of Shaw's works is (1) to expand all possibilities in terms of material and method; (2) to encourage a group of young people to imitate him and break away from old traditions.

Hallo Shaw

— Yang Xingzhi

Dear Shaw, what have you come to Shanghai for?

Are you here to record our colonial slaves?

Are you here to salute the British flag on the Huangpu River?

Are you here to hear the sound of Japanese guns killing people?

Are you here to praise our policy of non-resistance?

But I have to tell you:

Shanghai is not London, New York, or Paris,

Nor is it the red city of Leningrad,

The flags of Britain, America, Japan, and France fly proudly in the sky,

Clearly stating that China is just a colony,

Warships in the Huangpu River emit black smoke,

Coolies on the banks of the Huangpu River gasp for breath,

The blood and flesh of the weak support the authority of the strong,

Shanghai is such a semi-colonial city,

Do you feel that this is an "Unhappy drama"?

Let me tell you again:

What you said in Hong Kong is really outrageous!

Young people stuck out their tongues after hearing it,

Old people said "bullshit" after hearing it,

Perhaps some people even plan to be impolite to you.

When you arrive in Shanghai, don't talk nonsense again,

Because we don't understand humor,

And we are not allowed to speak casually,

I advise you to keep your mouth shut here,

In fact, why say more nonsense?

But, when you go back,

You have to bring back good news!

Just say:

China is not beyond salvation,

The waters of the Huangpu River will one day surge,

Washing away the darkness and authority of the earth!

Talking About Shaw (Continued)

— Lin Yutang

2. Shaw's Conch Shell

The merit of his attitude can be proved by the following paragraphs. Herris satirized Shaw, saying that while Shaw expressed hatred for the United States, he completely copied American advertising methods.

"Shaw's initial propaganda was just the usual method. From the beginning, he shouted, 'Give me big carts and bugles,' but now big carts and bugles are no longer popular, so he shouted, 'Give me radio and the screen.'" When he was young and debated with others, he knew how to attach himself to elegance, so that everyone associated him with the name of a certain celebrity. I remember once when he was debating with Heinemann, he stood up and said, "Marxism is as dead as mutton. I, Shaw, killed him.'"

So Herris has the following wonderful satirical passage: "He (Shaw) was the first to recognize the propaganda use of sound films... At this point, his lifetime of training in lecturing gave him a great advantage. He imitated Mussolini (translator's note: I saw this movie with my own eyes) and even imitated Shaw himself, which proves that he is a very great performer, even to the extreme of impersonation; however, it seems that what he was waving the flag and shouting against when he was writing plays in middle age was impersonation. He can even criticize the merits of his acting skills, and from sound films he saw that he was getting old and his mouth was gradually becoming unsightly. From then on, he switched to radio, which could broadcast his voice around the world without raising the issue of his personal curves."

Anyone who has read the preface to the play Caesar and Cleopatra remembers that Shaw raised a question: Beher then Shakespeari? (Is Shaw better than Shakespeare?) In 1896, Shaw wrote a review of Shakespeare's play (when the London Lyceum Theatre was playing Cymbiline), he said: "Except for Homer, no famous writer in ancient times, including Scott, is as despised by me as Shakespeare, when I compare his mind with my own. The degree of impatience I have with him sometimes makes me feel like simply digging up his corpse and throwing stones at him, because I know that Shakespeare and the group of people who worship him can only understand this kind of visible insult."

But remember that Shaw also said somewhere that "he is the most under-advertised person in the world." This is one of Shaw's conch shells. (To be continued)

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

My Personal Eight Grand Aspirations

— Wu

Now China has reached the time for everyone to swear oaths. Not only must oaths be sworn at meetings, but individuals also seem to swear oaths as well. The size of the oath is not restricted, only that it be made sincerely, because sincerity is the key.

Indeed, at present it is a time of chaos and war, with everyone from top to bottom terrified, and the true emperor is not yet born. Just as the three emperors of heaven, earth, and man have created a divine ox carriage, it was unfortunately all caught by Chairman Han, who does not follow the times, and then "dismissed with a smile." If things continue like this, it will certainly not end well. Therefore, the rise and fall of the world is the responsibility of every individual. We, the heavily sinful beings, must take this opportunity to make vows and swear oaths. When else? So I have eight grand aspirations. (1) I wish that all schools would be turned into dance halls. Since there are volunteer soldiers, we must also find ways to raise donations to help them, and the only way to raise donations is through dancing to have miraculous effects. Seeing that the existing dance halls are not enough, I wish to rebuild the schools, because reading to save the country has not shown unexpected effectiveness so far.

(2) I wish that all Chinese people would become artists. However, saving the country through art is no less effective than dancing. Unfortunately, there are still too few artists in China. It would be best if all Chinese people were artists, writers, and appreciators, everywhere. Then China would naturally be saved.

(3) I wish that all beings would obtain Prajna Paramita. However, some masters also say that China's demise is indeed due to the deep sins of all beings, so there should be several more meritorious ceremonies to allow all beings to finally obtain Prajna Paramita.

(4) I wish that all Chinese people would have a conscience. Of course, saving the country with a conscience is the most effective. If all Chinese people had a conscience, then the market for domestic goods would also be three times as profitable. The country would be saved without having to be saved.

(5) I wish that China's wheat would not be enough to meet the demand. It is said that because Chinese wheat is indeed not enough to meet the demand, and in order to regulate the people's food supply, Australian wheat must be transported to replace it. Moreover, Australian wheat is cheap and of good quality, so Chinese wheat should have poor harvests every year.

(6) I wish for floods every year. Because no dikes are being repaired this year, American wheat is not willing to be sold on credit. In order to provide relief to disaster victims, there should be floods every year.

(7) I wish that all rice paddies would be planted with poppies. If there is a good harvest, it will turn into a disaster. In order to prevent disasters, poppies should be planted instead, to enrich the country and increase its financial resources.

(8) I wish that all university students would have airplanes. Some people say that the reason why Peking University students want to "escape exams" and "have early holidays" is because they cannot each have an airplane. Well said! So I wish that university students would not have airplanes, so that they can scatter after danger, so as not to be scolded as "leaving a stink for ten thousand years."

The above are my eight grand aspirations. May heaven and earth truly witness these words.

Who Pities

Silken gowns and official hats all day idle, his determination to endure hardship is different from ordinary people, who pities the days of national destruction and family demise, still taking the iceberg as Mount Tai.

Science

Poison Gas (Continued)

— Meng Fu

(2) Lewisite: Lewisite is also a type of mustard gas, and its properties are similar to mustard gas. It is a dark-colored oily liquid with a suffocating and irritating odor. It was invented by an American chemist during the late Great War and is also known as "Death Dew."

(C) Lacrimatory and Irritating Throat and Nose Agents

(1) Chloropicrin: This toxic substance is a colorless liquid, which, when vaporized, is five and a half times heavier than air and has very strong persistence. In addition to causing tears, it can also cause vomiting and irritation of the mucous membranes of the nose and throat.

(2) Chloroacetophenone: This toxic substance is a crystalline solid at room temperature. It can irritate the eyes and cause tearing, but the irritated eyes only need to be exposed to fresh air for a few minutes to return to normal. It is most suitable for police use.

(3) Dibromodimethyl ether: This is a colorless oily liquid. After vaporization, it is six times heavier than air and has weak toxicity. It only irritates the mucous membranes of the eyes and causes tears, similar to the above. Irritating throat and nose agents are mostly solid arsenic compounds, filled in explosive shells, which explode with the shells. They can be divided into extremely fine mists. Their characteristic is that they can pass through imperfect gas masks, forcing the enemy to remove the masks because of the irritation. Now, let me briefly describe them below:

(1) Diphenylchlorarsine: This toxic substance is a solid at room temperature. It has a fecal odor. When there is a concentration of 1/17,000 in the air, it can kill people immediately in one minute. Even at a concentration of 1/10,000,000, it can still irritate the mucous membranes of the throat and nose, like a fire, forcing people to remove the mask, and it can also cause vomiting.

(2) Diphenylcyanoarsine: Its toxicity is slightly the same as the former, but its properties are stronger.

(3) Diphenylaminechlorarsine: This toxic substance is called "Adamsite" in the American army. Its toxicity is intermediate between the first two, and its other properties are similar.

(D) Systemic Poisonous Agents

(1) Prussic acid (i.e., hydrocyanic acid): A colorless, transparent liquid with the odor of bitter almond oil. It can damage the central nervous system. If there is 0.6 grams of this toxic gas in one cubic meter of air, that is, at a concentration of 1/2000 in the air volume, breathing for one minute will immediately cause death.

(2) Carbon monoxide: The coal gas poisoning that we often hear about in winter is caused by this gas. Carbon monoxide is a colorless gas. If the concentration in the air reaches 1/10, one minute is enough to kill people. In wartime, it is not very important because it is too light and easily volatilizes and disappears.

The above various toxic substances are either immediate-acting or delayed-acting. Immediate-acting substances include phosgene and chloropicrin, while delayed-acting substances include mustard gas. The most harmful toxic substances are phosgene, diphosgene, and mustard gas. (The End)

A Frightening Adventure

— Geng

The bright spring sunshine has already sent the deathly, gloomy winter god to another world.

Mr. Ding, after eating lunch on Sunday, strolled back and forth in X Park, shaking his "stick." He saw a girl coming towards him, with bright red lips, a tender white face, eyes that sparkled with youthful beauty, and a charming and beautiful outfit—instantly Mr. Ding was softened into white iron, attracted to magnetism, and only followed her. Unexpectedly, the girl also glanced at him from time to time, and finally, without prior agreement, they both sat on a bench under the cypress trees, chatted casually, and then seized the opportunity to move elsewhere.

"You're really bad. You insisted on entangling me here. Is your surname really Shuangmu Lin? Like Ru Fu? Where did you make a fortune?" They had just moved from the park to a magnificent hotel.

"It's really Shuangmu Lin, named Mei Xi, and I'm teaching at an art school now," Mr. Ding fabricated a fake name.

"With your elegant demeanor, I recognized you as a member of the upper class long ago."

"May I ask for the lady's name?"

"Eh! Didn't I tell you, when the time is right, you will naturally know." Then she yawned.

"Madam! Excuse my presumption, I want to ask you for a small favor..." His voice slightly trembled; and he reached out to stroke her pearl-like, jade-white wrists.

"You're too reckless! How can there be such a cheap thing in the world?" The lady suddenly left the sofa like a swift, opened the door, and pretended to escape.

"Ah! You misunderstand my intentions, come in and talk again, so as not to arouse the suspicion of the waiters."

"I said you're really bad, you still don't admit it?" she said, as if she were angry but not really. Then, with a "bang," she closed the door. With a slight smile, she went to the dressing table, pursing her lips and thinking silently, as if something were uncomfortable.

"Please forgive me..." He was confused, so he had to accompany her with respect and caution. But "fortune favors the bold," and fortune and romance naturally favor the bold even more. From then on, how Mr. Ding used all his energy to push this "good thing" forward? Only God knows what happened! Returning home with a sense of exhaustion, Mr. Ding answered the phone, but he denied in a pretending manner that there was such a person. It turned out that when they were enjoying the so-called "ripe time" of romance, he suddenly noticed that the girl had a gold chain necklace around her neck, and the jade pendant in the middle had the four words "X Hua Xiuying" engraved on it. Later,

Page 22

after inquiring, he found out that she was the famous Mr. X's fourth concubine. He almost got into a life-threatening disaster, so how could he dare not avoid it as soon as possible?

The Unemployed Professional

— Yu Lun

Who says Lu Xulun is not a typical college student?

He has paid the tuition and miscellaneous fees of one hundred and twenty-four yuan; a small teak desk, a rattan chair, and a few pieces of luggage have been transported to the dormitory of XX University. He has also put on a suit that is half new and not too old. Really, he is a newcomer in college.

Isn't reading a kind of profession? Moreover, college students are considered to be the upper class of society? So isn't a college student an unemployed person?

However, Lu Xulun is an unemployed person. The reason why he is a college student is because he is unemployed.

One hundred and twenty-four yuan is simply nothing in the eyes of the parents of some college students, just a matter of moving their hand and signing a check.

"Annoying! Such a piecemeal amount. Fill in two hundred yuan for me! You can take the rest for your own use."

Maybe those parents said that.

But one hundred and twenty-four yuan was decided by Lu Xulun's father after three or four nights of thinking.

"A Xu's position is hard to find; after the war, all industries are declining, and agencies everywhere are clamoring to lay off employees. If he has nothing to do and stays at home all day, he won't be doing anything. Spend a hundred and dozens of yuan and let him study in college for half a year! Maybe he can gain more knowledge. Anyway, there is no need to sign a contract and must study for four years. Within half a year, maybe he can find a decent job. At that time, in addition to filling in the middle school graduation on his resume, he can also add that he studied at XX University."

After such thorough thinking, he prepaid his salary for the next month from the bank, paid the tuition for Xulun, and repeatedly instructed:

"I don't want you to wear a mortarboard, but you don't have a job right now, and you are idle every day, I'm afraid that improper behavior will occur. So I'll let you try the taste of being a college student for the time being. Maybe you will have to do something in two months, but it won't happen, the earliest will be half a year."

Knowing that studying in college for half a year is useless, Xulun didn't want to go, but he was unemployed and didn't have the ability to take away other people's jobs.

"If you don't want to, you have to be willing," he thought, and on February 6, he took on the job of unemployed professional.
