Shop Assistant Communications

The Attitude a Debtor Should Have

Mr. Editor:

I am a person who has not even graduated from elementary school. Last year, I was recommended by relatives and friends to work as an apprentice in a hardware store. This year, I was fortunate enough to be promoted to the position of accounting clerk. My own situation can be considered settled for the time being, but what about my family! Alas! My father's shipping business has suffered a setback and is even worse than before, resulting in many deficits. Recently, due to the matter of payment for goods, the plaintiff applied for mediation for the first time. Since my father was still out of town, he was unable to attend court. However, recently, a default judgment was made, the main text of which stated "The defendant shall immediately pay the plaintiff for the goods; the application for provisional execution is rejected, and the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant," etc. Furthermore, the appeal period is within twenty days. After the judgment was delivered to my home, but my father's ship was again out of town, and I am a layman in the law, so I can only ask you for advice, sir.

(1) After the appeal period has passed, and I am unable to pay off the debt, what will happen according to the law?

(2) What does the application for provisional execution mean?

(3) I am nineteen years old this year. Can I have the power to represent my father?

Please take the trouble to answer the above questions. Thank you very much.

Sincerely, Yang Eqing

X X X X X X X X

Editor's Note:

Business failure is a common occurrence. However, owing debts requires repayment, and since a deficit has already occurred, responsibility should naturally be taken. Even if the money cannot be produced immediately, one should step forward and publicly allocate all assets for repayment. If it is not enough, then establish a practical and feasible reorganization plan. Seek understanding from others. As the saying goes, "Grasp the clear thatch to walk easily," so that there is still room for re-establishing one's business in the future. If one evades in every possible way, the creditor will naturally be anxious, and the result will be resorting to law, which will ultimately not allow you to shirk responsibility. Moreover, after one's reputation is ruined, there will be no hope for the future. Regarding your father's matter, after the plaintiff applied for mediation, although he was not in Shanghai at the time, he should have stated the reason and requested an extension. Even if he did not understand such procedures, he should have gone to discuss settlement procedures after returning to Shanghai. According to the usual practice of ordinary courts, handling such cases, from applying for mediation to declaring the mediation unsuccessful, formally filing a lawsuit, and finally issuing a default judgment, takes at least four months or more. Therefore, there is plenty of room to conduct settlement negotiations. Why did he not think of this and delayed in every possible way, leading to a default judgment? Now that the case has been judged, if you disagree, you can only appeal; although the time limit for appeal is stipulated to be twenty days, you can also state the reason and request an extension. However, to be realistic, if you ask yourself and are sure that you owe someone debt, then the result of the appeal will only increase the burden of litigation costs. It would be better to give up the appeal and prepare for debt repayment. When the appeal period expires and you are unable to pay off the debt, then the plaintiff will naturally file a lawsuit requesting execution; the court can immediately approve it and seal up the property.

As for "provisional execution," it is a legal term, meaning that before the case is judged, the plaintiff, because he fears that the defendant may hide or destroy property, requests that the defendant's property be temporarily sealed. The difference from execution is that because the case has not been judged, if the original case cannot be established in the future, it can of course still be unsealed; moreover, the defendant can also request compensation for the losses suffered as a result. Therefore, when requesting provisional execution, the applicant must provide a considerable amount of security. As for Mr. Yang's involvement in his father's affairs, it is of course "meddling in accounts," so the matter of representation is really inappropriate; however, submitting a statement requesting an extension of the appeal period is beneficial.

Novel

A Family of Scholars (Continued from XXIII)

— Wang Zhongxian

"Did your mother get your consent for this marriage?"

Daiqiu sighed and said, "I told my mother a long time ago that she doesn't need to seek my consent for engagement matters anymore. I am willing to marry anyone. Whether he is as poor as a beggar, as ugly as a living ghost, or as old as a longevity star, I am willing to marry him. Marrying out is better than staying here."

Youzhong smiled and said, "These are words of resentment. Do you hate to leave your mother so early?"

"How can anyone be willing to leave my mother? If my mother remains a widow for the rest of her life, I am willing to remain unmarried for life and stay with her until she dies."

"Then, you hate me! How can I eliminate the hatred in your heart?"

Daiqiu said with a bitter smile, "What does it have to do with you? It's not your turn for me to hate you!" As she said this, her voice was choked. Youzhong wanted to say something more, but Ruohua was already calling his name outside.

Tomorrow is the day of great joy for the Xia family's second house. Lamps are hung and decorations are displayed, making it very lively. Sang Aqiang specially took a day off from work and cleared out the wall gate room to allow the Xia family to make arrangements. The Zhao family sent over the betrothal gifts, including pearls, diamonds, and jewelry, everything that was needed. The relatives and friends who saw it were all satisfied. In the afternoon, the coal merchant led a handsome young man in Western clothes to pay respects to the mother-in-law, and the relatives and friends again praised him one after another. Ruohua carefully scrutinized the son-in-law and found him more and more interesting.

(12) You are a murderer!

Today, the Xia family is even more lively than when Zhongnan held the funeral! All the related relatives have arrived, except for Xia Tai Tai's nephew Zheng Jiping. He felt unspeakable sadness in his heart and naturally could not bear to attend Miss Xia's wedding banquet. Ruohua was very dissatisfied with him because of the last incident and did not bother to think about him anymore.

Youzhong happily entertained the new son-in-law and introduced him to Miss Daiqiu. Daiqiu met her fiancé and was teased by the guests, which embarrassed her to the point of tears. Xia Lao Taoye, Bodong, saw her shy and hesitant posture and could not help but stroke his beard and laugh.

The evening banquet was over, and the new son-in-law wanted to get up and leave. Youzhong, in order to connect the feelings of the new in-laws, insisted on keeping the son-in-law to play cards. After eight rounds of cards, the guests had already dispersed, leaving only the two matchmakers dozing off and waiting. Ruohua also asked the son-in-law to have a midnight snack before letting him go back. The new son-in-law bid farewell and went out. Youzhong personally escorted him to the gate. The road was as dark as lacquer. The matchmakers accompanied the new son-in-law to the alley entrance to get on the carriage. After only taking a dozen steps, they suddenly heard a gunshot. A person fell in response to the sound. In an instant, people were in an uproar. The coachman at the alley entrance took a light and came in to illuminate. Everyone was shocked to see that the one who was shot was the new son-in-law!

The two matchmakers: Upon hearing the gunshot, they turned around and fled. Hearing the gunman running over, they were so frightened that they huddled together, daring not to look up. Hearing others exclaim, they walked over to take a look. In the dim light, they saw the new son-in-law lying in a pool of blood and were so frightened that they trembled all over. Their limbs were powerless. Someone blew a police whistle, summoning a newly awakened policeman into the alley. Seeing that a person had died, the sleepiness that had been clouding the cop was frightened away. Another whistle blared, summoning three or five patrol police to help. They took control of the people in the dark alley, asked about the situation, and then went to knock on the Xia family's gate. The tailor-secretary asked clearly before daring to open the door. They accompanied them in to knock on the inner gate. By the time Youzhong rushed outside, the new son-in-law's spirit had already left the ghost gate and drunk Meng Po soup. Youzhong still ordered the coachman to send the corpse to the hospital and sent a messenger to the Zhao family to report the news. The two matchmakers were taken into custody by the police, who said they were suspected of murder.
